# Meta-Harness Repository Guidance

Before planning or implementing a non-trivial enhancement, read
`docs/PROJECT_CHARTER.md` and state which product-loop stage and invariant the
change advances.

Use the charter as the repository's enhancement decision gate:

- preserve goal specification, generated-harness recommendation, managed
  rehearsal/correction, H/E/W learning, cross-harness `SolutionTemplate` reuse,
  and reproducible package/deploy/monitor/rollback as one coherent product loop;
- support versioned hybrid frontier/open-weight and pure open-weight portfolios;
  treat hosted model selection, routing, prompts, and inference parameters as
  `H`, trainable open checkpoints as `W`, and never conflate autonomous
  improvement with evaluator or deployment self-approval;
- treat code generation as a versioned, instrumented candidate surface;
- preserve evaluator non-self-approval, full-fidelity evidence, controlled
  attribution, bounded authority, human promotion, and exact rollback; and
- do not claim planned capabilities are implemented.

If a requested change conflicts with the charter or would redefine the project
mission, surface the conflict and require an explicit charter revision rather
than allowing implementation drift.

## Development Kanban (Linear team "Meta-Harness", `META`)

Coding-agent seats (Codex, Claude Code) coordinate development work through the
Linear team `Meta-Harness` in workspace `cha-personal`. Conventions:

- Pull only cards in **Ready**. Backlog cards are not claimable; only the
  coordinator qualifies a card and moves it to Ready.
- One card in progress per agent (one-card WIP). Claim by moving the card to
  **In Progress** and assigning yourself before editing anything.
- Advance states as work progresses: In Progress → Review → Verifying → Done.
  Use **Blocked** when stuck and say why; the coordinator triages.
- Comment evidence on the card at each transition: branch, commits, test
  output, review verdicts — artifacts, not assertions.
- Respect lane labels (`codex`, `claude-code`, `coordinator`): pick up only
  cards labeled for your seat unless the coordinator reassigns.
- Linear is the **visible development board only**, not the atomic claim
  authority. Single-winner claims, fencing, and path reservations belong to the
  Kanban control root / claim gateway (TASK-20260714-001/010). This is
  development-plane coordination; product runtime components (`Router`,
  `TaskExecutor`, `WorkflowEngine`) never touch development cards or receive
  Linear credentials.

## Independent Second-Opinion Review

Every non-trivial implementation must receive a frozen-diff second-opinion
review from **Pi using NeuralWatt GLM-5.2** before it advances from Review. The
implementing seat's self-review does not satisfy this gate.

- Freeze the exact review commit and base commit in the atomic card before
  dispatch. Review that immutable diff; do not review a moving worktree.
- Run Pi/GLM as a reviewer with read-only permissions. The bounded one-shot
  invocation is:

  ```bash
  pi --provider neuralwatt --model glm-5.2 \
    --permission-mode read-only \
    --tools read,grep,find,ls,bash \
    --no-session --print "<frozen-diff review brief>"
  ```

- The brief must identify the base and head commits, acceptance criteria,
  charter invariants, and test evidence. It must explicitly forbid edits and
  require file-and-line evidence for every finding.
- Require a verdict plus findings classified as P0, P1, P2, or P3. Preserve
  the review output verbatim in `.review-store/` and comment the artifact path,
  model, frozen commit, and dispositions on the Linear card.
- Any unresolved P0 or P1 blocks integration. The implementing seat must
  classify each substantive finding as `ACCEPT`, `ACCEPT-WITH-MOD`, `REJECT`,
  `DEFER`, or `NEEDS-EVIDENCE`, apply accepted fixes, rerun relevant tests, and
  request a fresh Pi/GLM review of the new frozen commit.
- If Pi, NeuralWatt, or GLM-5.2 is unavailable, leave the card in Review (or
  mark it Blocked with evidence). Never silently substitute self-review or
  claim independent approval.
- A separate coordinator remains responsible for integration, verification,
  and acceptance after the Pi/GLM gate passes.
# META-19 Build Spec — Promote shadow ContextEnvelope to the live prompt path

Card: `TASK-20260719-013` (Linear META-19). Frozen definition:
`.agents/meta19-definition.json`
(`sha256:3557334572665080c7d2ddd28af5bca5bf35f9d12aeeb983f04d972bd9b55d96`).
Worktree: `/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19`, branch
`dev/meta-19-live-context-envelope`, base `46c60fa`. Use the WORKTREE venv:
`/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/.venv/bin/pytest`.

## Outcome

The typed `ContextEnvelope` stops being a shadow sidecar and becomes the single
live assembler both worker families consume. Trust rules and secret redaction
apply to the bytes actually sent; the `ContextManifest` is journaled per attempt
as the authoritative "what did the model see" record. Divergence between
manifest and sent bytes is impossible by construction because the sent bytes are
DERIVED FROM the validated envelope, not observed after the fact.

## Current state (read these first)

- `src/metaharness/context/models.py` — frozen contracts (do not weaken).
  Trust enum at :52; evaluator-receipt-never-INSTRUCTION at :168-177;
  `ContextEnvelope` validators at :228; `ContextManifest` at :339 with
  `reconstruct_messages()` / `reconstruct_tool_schemas()`.
- `src/metaharness/context/assembly.py` — `fit_messages` (legacy fitter, :111),
  `fit_messages_with_receipt` (shadow observer, :246), redaction machinery
  (:148-193), `_message_contract` (:196) which infers section/trust from
  role — this inference direction is what promotion inverts: callers now
  DECLARE sections; messages are rendered from them.
- `src/metaharness/harness/local.py` — `_build_messages` (:41) ad-hoc concat;
  `_execute` loop (:183-249) runs the shadow observer per round, falls back to
  the legacy fitter on ANY assembler exception, emits
  `context.manifest.shadow` / `context.manifest.shadow_failed`.
- `src/metaharness/harness/coding.py` — `_render_prompt` (:273) ad-hoc concat
  into one flat prompt; no manifest at all today.
- `src/metaharness/observability/run_events.py` — `emit_run_event` is bound by
  `core/executor.py:214` to the attempt event stream (payloads get `{"n": …}`
  merged in), so a worker-side emit IS per-attempt journaling. No executor
  change is needed or allowed (not an owned path).
- Callers: ONLY `local.py` and `coding.py` build prompts. Nothing else calls
  `_build_messages` / `_render_prompt` / `fit_messages_with_receipt`.

## Stage 1 — live assembler (`src/metaharness/context/live.py` + exports)

New module `src/metaharness/context/live.py`:

1. `SectionDraft` (frozen pydantic, extra=forbid): the caller-declared input —
   `section_type: ContextSectionType`, `source_kind: ContextSourceKind`,
   `stable_id`, `trust: ContextTrust`, `sensitivity: Sensitivity`,
   `content: str`, plus optional `role` hint for message rendering
   (system/user/assistant/tool + `tool_call_id`). Keep it minimal — token
   counts and hashes are computed by the assembler, never declared.
2. `LiveContextViolation(Exception)` — typed, raised BEFORE any model call.
3. `assemble_live(drafts, *, budget_tokens, model_id, harness_version, tier,
   redaction_values, tool_schemas=None, policy_version="context-live-v1",
   …version bindings kwargs) -> LiveAssembly` where `LiveAssembly` (frozen)
   carries `messages` (chat list, redacted, fitted), `prompt` (flat string
   rendered from the same sections, for CLI workers), `envelope`, `manifest`.
   Pipeline order (deterministic, no wall-clock, no randomness):
   a. **Trust enforcement (fail closed).** Instruction slots =
      {SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS, RESPONSE_CONTRACT, TOOL_SCHEMAS}. A draft whose
      `section_type` is an instruction slot MUST carry trust INSTRUCTION; a
      draft with trust UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE or GENERATED_SUMMARY may never
      occupy one. EVALUATOR_RECEIPT sources never carry INSTRUCTION (already
      enforced by `ContextSourceRef`; surface it as `LiveContextViolation`
      not a bare pydantic error). Violations raise `LiveContextViolation`.
   b. **Redaction on live content.** Reuse `_redact` /
      `_BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS` against each draft's content BEFORE fitting;
      the redacted text is what enters sections, messages, prompt, and
      manifest alike (single source of truth ⇒ no shadow/live divergence).
   c. **Budget fitting.** Reuse the existing deterministic head/tail digest
      (`digest_text`) semantics per section against
      `allocate_section_budgets`; protected edge sections
      (SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS, RESPONSE_CONTRACT) are never omitted (the
      models.py validator already forbids it). Record per-section
      `CompressionReceipt`s honestly.
   d. **Envelope + manifest.** Build `ContextSection`s from the fitted
      sections, then the `ContextEnvelope` and `ContextManifest` exactly as
      `assembly.py` does today (reuse helpers where practical —
      `_make_envelope`, hashing). Messages = rendered from sections; the
      manifest's `reconstruct_messages()` MUST equal the returned `messages`
      byte-for-byte (this is the divergence-impossible property; test it).
   e. **Flat prompt rendering.** `prompt` = the same sections joined in
      ordering-priority order with the same headings local/coding use today
      (Boundaries:/Constraints:/Inputs:/output-schema phrasing preserved so
      prompt content parity holds where no redaction/violation applies).
4. Keep `fit_messages` and `fit_messages_with_receipt` exported and unchanged
   (other callers/tests rely on them; `fit_messages` remains the tool-round
   refit primitive if needed). Export the new names from
   `context/__init__.py`.

## Stage 2 — `harness/local.py` consumes the assembler

- `_build_messages` is replaced by a function that DECLARES `SectionDraft`s:
  system prompt (+persona) → SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS / PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS /
  INSTRUCTION; boundaries + output-schema directive → RESPONSE_CONTRACT /
  RESPONSE_CONTRACT / INSTRUCTION; objective → TASK_CONTRACT / GOAL /
  INSTRUCTION; task inputs → WORKFLOW_STATE / LIVE_RUN_STATE /
  UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE (inputs are data, not instructions — this is a deliberate
  trust correction; render them in the user message under the existing
  "Inputs:" heading).
- Each round of the tool loop: append assistant turns (LIVE_RUN_STATE /
  UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE) and tool observations (IMMUTABLE_ARTIFACT /
  UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE) as new drafts and re-run `assemble_live`; send
  `assembly.messages`.
- Emit ONE non-shadow event per round: kind `context.manifest`, payload
  `{"schema_version": 1, "shadow": False, "task_id", "round",
  "live_messages_hash": content_hash(sent messages), "manifest": …}`.
  Executor sink binding adds the attempt number. Telemetry sink failure must
  not fail the model call (keep the try/except around emit ONLY).
- **Failure semantics change (the point of the card):**
  `LiveContextViolation` and redaction/contract failures PROPAGATE (fail
  closed; no model call, no legacy fallback). The old fall-back-to-legacy
  behavior and `context.manifest.shadow*` events are removed. Genuine
  infrastructure impossibilities do not exist here — assembly is pure
  computation; any exception is a contract violation and fails the attempt
  loudly (WorkerResult.error via the BaseRunner error path, as any raise does
  today).
- Header `Authorization` keeps the real api_key (transport, not context);
  `redaction_values=[api_key]` scrubs it from CONTENT.

## Stage 3 — `harness/coding.py` consumes the assembler

- `_render_prompt` declares the same drafts (objective TASK_CONTRACT/GOAL/
  INSTRUCTION; "Constraints:" → RESPONSE_CONTRACT/RESPONSE_CONTRACT/
  INSTRUCTION; inputs → WORKFLOW_STATE/LIVE_RUN_STATE/UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE;
  output-schema print-directive → RESPONSE_CONTRACT trust INSTRUCTION merged
  with constraints or a separate draft with a distinct stable_id) and calls
  `assemble_live` with the CLI worker's tier budget; the CLI receives
  `assembly.prompt`.
- `system_prompt` (passed via CLI flag, not prompt text) is DECLARED as a
  SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS draft so it appears in the manifest, but the rendered
  flat prompt excludes it (it travels via `--append-system-prompt`); mark the
  section's message-rendering role accordingly. The manifest must still
  attest it (what the model saw includes it).
- Emit `context.manifest` once per attempt (same payload shape; `"round": 0`).
- Same fail-closed semantics; no fallback rendering.

## Stage 4 — tests (owned test files only)

New/updated tests, each citing META-19:

1. **Trust violation, no model call**: a task/system_prompt path that declares
   untrusted content into an instruction slot raises `LiveContextViolation`;
   with an injected httpx client (local) / stub binary (coding), assert the
   endpoint was NEVER hit.
2. **Redaction on sent bytes**: seed a secret (api_key value + `sk-…` pattern)
   into task inputs; capture the actual request body via injected client and
   assert `[REDACTED]` appears and the raw secret does not; assert manifest
   `redaction_count` agrees.
3. **Divergence impossible**: `manifest.reconstruct_messages()` equals the
   messages the client actually received (hash equality on canonical JSON).
4. **Journal answers attempt N**: bind a run-event sink, run ≥2 rounds (tool
   loop), assert one `context.manifest` event per round with
   `live_messages_hash` matching each round's sent messages; assert
   `shadow` is False and no `context.manifest.shadow` event exists anymore.
5. **Content parity**: for a representative no-secret, no-violation task, the
   assembled user/system text contains the same objective/boundaries/inputs
   content the legacy builders produced (heading-level parity, not
   byte-identity across the whole list).
6. **Determinism**: same inputs → identical envelope/manifest hashes.
7. **Coding worker**: flat prompt contains the same sections; manifest
   emitted; stub-binary test proves prompt content.
8. Update the tests that assert the superseded shadow-only contract
   (`tests/test_context.py:244-330` region: shadow event shape, byte-identity
   fallback, sink-failure fallback) to the new live contract. Sink-failure
   tolerance (telemetry cannot fail the call) KEEPS a test — only the
   legacy-fallback-on-assembler-error assertions are superseded. Cite META-19
   in each changed test's docstring.
9. `tests/adversarial/test_memory_skill_boundaries.py` mentions shadow for
   MEMORY (META-6) — that broker stays shadow; do NOT touch memory-broker
   semantics. Only context-path assertions change.

## Hard boundaries (from the frozen card — violations are stop conditions)

  `harness/coding.py`, `tests/test_context.py`, `tests/test_local_worker.py`,
  `tests/test_coding.py`, `tests/test_harness.py`, `tests/adversarial`.
- No new authority: no evaluator/merge/promotion/deployment/credential grants;
  memory broker stays shadow; H/E/W frozen; selflearn untouched.
- Do not weaken `models.py` validators or delete META-4/5/6 assertions except
  the explicitly superseded shadow-only ones (cite META-19 at each).
- Determinism: no wall-clock, no randomness in assembly.
- Do not commit; report per stage with test counts + deviations.

    13	    """A segment equal to '..' (forward or backslash separated) is path traversal."""

    16	    return ".." in value.replace("\\", "/").split("/")

    23	    return json.dumps(value, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":"))

    26	def content_hash(value: Any) -> str:
    27	    material = value if isinstance(value, str) else canonical_json(value)
    28	    return "sha256:" + hashlib.sha256(material.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

    86	class ContextVersionBindings(FrozenModel):
    87	    """The immutable evidence/lineage tuple for one context assembly.
    88	
    89	    Cross-axis convention (documented): a `harness_version` self-declaring
    90	    a breaking schema change (a '-breaking-' segment in the version string)
    91	    must not bind a non-None `memory_snapshot_version` or
    92	    `evidence_snapshot_version`. Reusing those snapshots across a breaking
    93	    bump silently passes the per-axis checks today; the convention forces
    94	    callers to pick a fresh (or explicitly-None) snapshot pair, with a
    95	    future reconciliation marker providing the opt-in to reuse.
    96	    """
    97	
    98	    model_portfolio_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
    99	    harness_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   100	    evaluator_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   101	    weight_snapshot_version: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   102	    memory_snapshot_version: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   103	    evidence_snapshot_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   104	    candidate_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   105	    parent_candidate_version: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   106	
   107	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   108	    def validate_lineage(self) -> "ContextVersionBindings":
   109	        if self.parent_candidate_version == self.candidate_version:
   110	            raise ValueError("candidate and parent versions must differ")
   111	        if "breaking" in self.harness_version.split("-"):
   112	            if self.memory_snapshot_version is not None or self.evidence_snapshot_version is not None:
   113	                raise ValueError(
   114	                    "harness_version declares a breaking schema change "
   115	                    "('-breaking-' segment); memory_snapshot_version and "
   116	                    "evidence_snapshot_version must be None rather than "
   117	                    "reusing prior-version snapshots across the bump "
   118	                    "(future reconciliation marker: not yet supported)"
   119	                )
   120	        return self
   121	
   122	
   123	class ContextScope(FrozenModel):
   124	    project_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   125	    run_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   126	    task_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   127	    attempt_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   128	    lineage_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   129	
   130	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   131	    def validate_nesting(self) -> "ContextScope":
   132	        if self.task_id is not None and self.run_id is None:
   133	            raise ValueError("task_id requires run_id")
   134	        if self.attempt_id is not None and self.task_id is None:
   135	            raise ValueError("attempt_id requires task_id")
   136	        return self
   137	
   138	
   139	class ContextSourceRef(FrozenModel):
   140	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   141	    source_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   142	    kind: ContextSourceKind
   143	    scope: ContextScope
   144	    trust: ContextTrust
   145	    content_hash: str | None = Field(default=None, pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   146	    high_water_mark: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   147	    selection_reason: str = Field(min_length=1)
   148	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   149	    fetchable: bool
   150	    artifact_ref: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   151	
   152	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   153	    def validate_identity_and_fetch(self) -> "ContextSourceRef":
   154	        if (self.content_hash is None) == (self.high_water_mark is None):
   155	            raise ValueError("exactly one of content_hash or high_water_mark is required")
   156	        if self.fetchable != (self.artifact_ref is not None):
   157	            raise ValueError("fetchable sources require exactly one artifact_ref")
   158	        if _contains_traversal_segment(self.source_id):
   159	            raise ValueError(
   160	                "source_id must not contain path-traversal sequences "
   161	                "(e.g. '..' / '..\\..\\' segments)"
   162	            )
   163	        if self.artifact_ref is not None and _contains_traversal_segment(self.artifact_ref):
   164	            raise ValueError(
   165	                "artifact_ref must not contain path-traversal sequences "
   166	                "(e.g. '..' / '..\\..\\' segments)"
   167	            )
   168	        if (
   169	            self.kind is ContextSourceKind.EVALUATOR_RECEIPT
   170	            and self.trust is ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION
   171	        ):
   172	            raise ValueError(
   173	                "evaluator_receipt sources are evidence and may never "
   174	                "carry INSTRUCTION trust (no self-promotion to instruction "
   175	                "authority)"
   176	            )
   177	        return self
   178	
   179	
   180	class ContextSection(FrozenModel):
   181	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   182	    section_type: ContextSectionType
   183	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   184	    source: ContextSourceRef
   185	    source_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   186	    trust: ContextTrust
   187	    content: str
   188	    original_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   189	    selected_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   190	    compressed_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   191	    budget_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   192	    ordering_priority: int = Field(ge=0)
   193	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   194	    redaction_markers: tuple[str, ...] = ()
   195	    compression_action: CompressionAction = CompressionAction.NONE
   196	    omission_reason: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   197	    retrieval_score: float | None = None
   198	
   199	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   200	    def validate_provenance_and_counts(self) -> "ContextSection":
   201	        if self.source.content_hash is not None and self.source_hash != self.source.content_hash:
   202	            raise ValueError("source_hash must match source.content_hash")
   203	        if self.trust != self.source.trust:
   204	            raise ValueError("section trust must match source trust")
   205	        if self.sensitivity != self.source.sensitivity:
   206	            raise ValueError("section sensitivity must match source sensitivity")
   207	        if self.selected_tokens > self.original_tokens:
   208	            raise ValueError("selected token count cannot exceed original")
   209	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.NONE:
   210	            if self.omission_reason is not None:
   211	                raise ValueError("uncompressed sections cannot have an omission reason")
   212	            if self.compressed_tokens != self.selected_tokens:
   213	                raise ValueError("uncompressed token counts must match")
   214	        elif self.omission_reason is None:
   215	            raise ValueError("compression or omission requires a reason")
   216	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED and self.content:
   217	            raise ValueError("omitted sections cannot retain content")
   218	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED and self.compressed_tokens != 0:
   219	            raise ValueError("omitted sections must have zero rendered tokens")
   220	        if self.section_type in {
   221	            ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   222	            ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   223	        } and self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED:
   224	            raise ValueError("protected edge sections cannot be omitted")
   225	        return self
   226	
   227	
   228	class ContextEnvelope(FrozenModel):
   229	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   230	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   231	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   232	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   233	    sections: tuple[ContextSection, ...]
   234	    content_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   235	
   236	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   237	    def validate_hash_and_order(self) -> "ContextEnvelope":
   238	        if len({section.stable_id for section in self.sections}) != len(self.sections):
   239	            raise ValueError("section stable_id values must be unique")
   240	        priorities = [section.ordering_priority for section in self.sections]
   241	        if priorities != list(range(len(self.sections))):
   242	            raise ValueError("sections must have unique contiguous priorities")
   243	        project_ids = {section.source.scope.project_id for section in self.sections}
   244	        if len(project_ids) > 1:
   245	            raise ValueError(
   246	                "envelope sections must share a single source scope "
   247	                "project_id (no cross-project scope bleed); got "
   248	                f"{sorted(project_ids)}"
   249	            )
   250	        identity_by_source_id: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
   251	        for section in self.sections:
   252	            mode = "pinned" if section.source.content_hash is not None else "live"
   253	            identity_by_source_id.setdefault(section.source.source_id, set()).add(mode)
   254	        for source_id, modes in identity_by_source_id.items():
   255	            if len(modes) > 1:
   256	                raise ValueError(
   257	                    f"envelope sections sharing source_id={source_id!r} mix "
   258	                    "pinned (content_hash) and live (high_water_mark) identity "
   259	                    "without an explicit reconciliation marker (future "
   260	                    "marker: not yet supported)"
   261	                )
   262	        material = self.model_dump(mode="json", exclude={"content_hash"})
   263	        if self.content_hash != content_hash(material):
   264	            raise ValueError("envelope content_hash mismatch")
   265	        return self
   266	
   267	
   268	class CompressionReceipt(FrozenModel):
   269	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   270	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   271	    action: CompressionAction
   272	    before_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   273	    after_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   274	    original_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   275	    final_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   276	    reason: str = Field(min_length=1)
   277	    fidelity_loss_estimate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
   278	
   279	    @model_validator(mode="before")
   280	    @classmethod
   281	    def _fill_fidelity_loss_estimate(cls, data: Any) -> Any:
   282	        if not isinstance(data, dict) or "fidelity_loss_estimate" in data:
   283	            return data
   284	        action = data.get("action")
   285	        original = data.get("original_tokens") or 0
   286	        final = data.get("final_tokens") or 0
   287	        if action is CompressionAction.NONE:
   288	            data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = 0.0
   289	            return data
   290	        if original <= 0:
   291	            data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = 0.0 if final <= 0 else 1.0
   292	            return data
   293	        loss = 1.0 - (final / original)
   294	        if loss < 0.0:
   295	            loss = 0.0
   296	        elif loss > 1.0:
   297	            loss = 1.0
   298	        data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = loss
   299	        return data
   300	
   301	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   302	    def validate_change(self) -> "CompressionReceipt":
   303	        changed = self.before_hash != self.after_hash
   304	        if (self.action is CompressionAction.NONE) == changed:
   305	            raise ValueError("compression action must agree with before/after hashes")
   306	        return self
   307	
   308	
   309	class ContextManifestEntry(FrozenModel):
   310	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   311	    surface: Literal["message", "tool_schemas"]
   312	    payload_json: str = Field(min_length=2)
   313	    source_kind: ContextSourceKind
   314	    trust: ContextTrust
   315	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   316	    source_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   317	    selected_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   318	    redacted: bool = False
   319	
   320	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   321	    def validate_payload(self) -> "ContextManifestEntry":
   322	        try:
   323	            payload = json.loads(self.payload_json)
   324	        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
   325	            raise ValueError("payload_json must be canonical JSON") from exc
   326	        if self.payload_json != canonical_json(payload):
   327	            raise ValueError("payload_json must be canonical JSON")
   328	        if self.surface == "message" and not isinstance(payload, dict):
   329	            raise ValueError("message payload must be an object")
   330	        if self.surface == "tool_schemas" and not (
   331	            isinstance(payload, list) and all(isinstance(item, dict) for item in payload)
   332	        ):
   333	            raise ValueError("tool_schemas payload must be an object array")
   334	        if self.selected_hash != content_hash(payload):
   335	            raise ValueError("selected_hash must attest payload_json")
   336	        return self
   337	
   338	
   339	class ContextManifest(FrozenModel):
   340	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   341	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   342	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   343	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   344	    envelope_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   345	    redacted_envelope_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   346	    redacted_envelope_json: str = Field(min_length=2)
   347	    entries: tuple[ContextManifestEntry, ...]
   348	    compression_receipts: tuple[CompressionReceipt, ...]
   349	    source_candidates_considered: tuple[str, ...]
   350	    visibility_decisions: tuple[str, ...]
   351	    deliberate_omissions: tuple[str, ...]
   352	    artifact_refs: tuple[str, ...]
   353	    budget_used_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   354	    budget_limit_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   355	    redaction_count: int = Field(ge=0)
   356	    manifest_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   357	
   358	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   359	    def validate_manifest_hash(self) -> "ContextManifest":
   360	        if len(self.entries) != len(self.compression_receipts):
   361	            raise ValueError("each manifest entry requires a compression receipt")
   362	        if len({entry.stable_id for entry in self.entries}) != len(self.entries):
   363	            raise ValueError("manifest entry stable_id values must be unique")
   364	        if tuple(entry.stable_id for entry in self.entries) != tuple(
   365	            receipt.stable_id for receipt in self.compression_receipts
   366	        ):
   367	            raise ValueError("manifest entries and compression receipts must align")
   368	        material = self.model_dump(mode="json", exclude={"manifest_hash"})
   369	        if self.manifest_hash != content_hash(material):
   370	            raise ValueError("manifest_hash mismatch")
   371	        try:
   372	            redacted_envelope = json.loads(self.redacted_envelope_json)
   373	        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
   374	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_json must be canonical JSON") from exc
   375	        if self.redacted_envelope_json != canonical_json(redacted_envelope):
   376	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_json must be canonical JSON")
   377	        if self.redacted_envelope_hash != content_hash(redacted_envelope):
   378	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_hash mismatch")
   379	        envelope = ContextEnvelope.model_validate(redacted_envelope)
   380	        if envelope.content_hash != redacted_envelope.get("content_hash"):
   381	            raise ValueError("redacted envelope content hash mismatch")
   382	        required_artifact_refs = {
   383	            section.source.artifact_ref
   384	            for section in envelope.sections
   385	            if section.source.fetchable and section.source.artifact_ref is not None
   386	        }
   387	        provided_artifact_refs = set(self.artifact_refs)
   388	        missing = required_artifact_refs - provided_artifact_refs
   389	        if missing:
   390	            raise ValueError(
   391	                "artifact_refs must include every fetchable source's "
   392	                f"artifact_ref; missing: {sorted(missing)}"
   393	            )
   394	        return self
   395	
   396	    def reconstruct_messages(self) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   397	        return [json.loads(entry.payload_json) for entry in self.entries if entry.surface == "message"]
   398	
   399	    def reconstruct_tool_schemas(self) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   400	        schemas = [json.loads(entry.payload_json) for entry in self.entries if entry.surface == "tool_schemas"]
   401	        return [schema for group in schemas for schema in group]
   402	
   403	    def reconstruct_redacted_envelope(self) -> ContextEnvelope:
   404	        return ContextEnvelope.model_validate_json(self.redacted_envelope_json)
     1	"""Legacy-compatible fitting plus deterministic typed shadow receipts."""
     2	from __future__ import annotations
     3	
     4	import re
     5	from typing import Any, Iterable
     6	
     7	from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict
     8	
     9	from metaharness.context.models import (
    10	    CompressionAction,
    11	    CompressionReceipt,
    12	    ContextEnvelope,
    13	    ContextManifest,
    14	    ContextManifestEntry,
    15	    ContextScope,
    16	    ContextSection,
    17	    ContextSectionType,
    18	    ContextSourceKind,
    19	    ContextSourceRef,
    20	    ContextTrust,
    21	    ContextVersionBindings,
    22	    Sensitivity,
    23	    canonical_json,
    24	    content_hash,
    25	)
    26	from metaharness.core.types import Tier
    27	from metaharness.tools.registry import digest_text

    29	TIER_CONTEXT_BUDGET: dict[Tier, int] = {
    30	    Tier.SMALL: 8_000,
    31	    Tier.MID: 16_000,
    32	    Tier.FRONTIER: 32_000,
    33	}
    34	GENERATION_RESERVE = 0.25
    35	
    36	TIER_SECTION_WEIGHTS: dict[Tier, dict[ContextSectionType, int]] = {
    37	    Tier.SMALL: {
    38	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS: 24,
    39	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT: 24,
    40	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS: 8,
    41	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    42	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 10,
    43	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 7,
    44	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 4,
    45	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 8,
    46	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 5,
    47	    },
    48	    Tier.MID: {
    49	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS: 20,
    50	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT: 21,
    51	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS: 9,
    52	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    53	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 14,
    54	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 9,
    55	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 5,
    56	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 7,
    57	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 5,
    58	    },
    59	    Tier.FRONTIER: {
    60	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS: 16,
    61	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT: 18,
    62	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS: 10,
    63	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    64	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 18,
    65	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 11,
    66	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 7,
    67	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 6,
    68	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 4,
    69	    },
    70	}
    71	
    72	
    73	def estimate_tokens(text: str) -> int:
    74	    return len(text) // 4 + 1
    75	
    76	
    77	def messages_tokens(messages: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> int:
    78	    return sum(estimate_tokens(str(message.get("content") or "")) for message in messages)
    79	
    80	
    81	def budget_for(tier: Tier, override: int | None = None) -> int:
    82	    budget = override or TIER_CONTEXT_BUDGET.get(tier, 8_000)
    83	    return int(budget * (1 - GENERATION_RESERVE))
    84	
    85	
    86	def allocate_section_budgets(
    87	    section_types: list[ContextSectionType],
    88	    budget_tokens: int,
    89	    tier: Tier,
    90	) -> list[int]:
    91	    """Allocate the whole budget by tier using deterministic largest remainder."""
    92	    if budget_tokens < 0:
    93	        raise ValueError("budget_tokens must be nonnegative")
    94	    if not section_types:
    95	        return []
    96	    weights = TIER_SECTION_WEIGHTS[tier]
    97	    raw_weights = [weights[section_type] for section_type in section_types]
    98	    total_weight = sum(raw_weights)
    99	    numerators = [budget_tokens * weight for weight in raw_weights]
   100	    allocations = [numerator // total_weight for numerator in numerators]
   101	    remaining = budget_tokens - sum(allocations)
   102	    order = sorted(
   103	        range(len(section_types)),
   104	        key=lambda index: (-(numerators[index] % total_weight), index),
   105	    )
   106	    for index in order[:remaining]:
   107	        allocations[index] += 1
   108	    return allocations
   109	
   110	
   111	def fit_messages(messages: list[dict[str, Any]], budget_tokens: int) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   112	    """Preserve the pre-contract fitting behavior exactly for existing callers."""
   113	    if messages_tokens(messages) <= budget_tokens:
   114	        return messages
   115	    result = [dict(message) for message in messages]
   116	    prunable = [
   117	        index
   118	        for index, message in enumerate(result)
   119	        if not (index == 0 and message.get("role") == "system")
   120	        and index != len(result) - 1
   121	    ]
   122	
   123	    def priority(index: int) -> tuple[int, int]:
   124	        role_rank = 0 if result[index].get("role") == "tool" else 1
   125	        return role_rank, -len(str(result[index].get("content") or ""))
   126	
   127	    for index in sorted(prunable, key=priority):
   128	        if messages_tokens(result) <= budget_tokens:
   129	            break
   130	        text = str(result[index].get("content") or "")
   131	        overshoot = messages_tokens(result) - budget_tokens
   132	        target_chars = max(400, len(text) - overshoot * 4 - 200)
   133	        if target_chars < len(text):
   134	            result[index]["content"] = digest_text(text, target_chars)
   135	    return result
   136	
   137	
   138	class ContextFitReceipt(BaseModel):
   139	    """Internal sidecar: live messages plus the safe durable shadow receipt."""
   140	
   141	    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid", frozen=True)
   142	    messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   143	    redacted_messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   144	    envelope: ContextEnvelope
   145	    manifest: ContextManifest
   146	
   147	
   148	_BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS = (
   149	    re.compile(r"\bsk-[A-Za-z0-9_-]{8,}\b"),
   150	    re.compile(r"(?i)(authorization\s*:\s*bearer\s+)[^\s,;]+"),
   151	)
   152	
   153	
   154	def _redact_string(value: str, redaction_values: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[str, int]:
   155	    redacted = value
   156	    count = 0
   157	    for secret in redaction_values:
   158	        occurrences = redacted.count(secret)
   159	        if occurrences:
   160	            redacted = redacted.replace(secret, "[REDACTED]")
   161	            count += occurrences
   162	    for pattern in _BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS:
   163	        def replace(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
   164	            nonlocal count
   165	            count += 1
   166	            prefix = match.group(1) if match.lastindex else ""
   167	            return prefix + "[REDACTED]"
   168	
   169	        redacted = pattern.sub(replace, redacted)
   170	    return redacted, count
   171	
   172	
   173	def _redact(value: Any, redaction_values: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[Any, int]:
   174	    if isinstance(value, str):
   175	        return _redact_string(value, redaction_values)
   176	    if isinstance(value, list):
   177	        output, total = [], 0
   178	        for item in value:
   179	            clean, count = _redact(item, redaction_values)
   180	            output.append(clean)
   181	            total += count
   182	        return output, total
   183	    if isinstance(value, dict):
   184	        output, total = {}, 0
   185	        for key in sorted(value):
   186	            clean_key, key_count = _redact_string(key, redaction_values)
   187	            if clean_key != key:
   188	                clean_key = f"[REDACTED_KEY_{len(output)}]"
   189	            clean, count = _redact(value[key], redaction_values)
   190	            output[clean_key] = clean
   191	            total += key_count + count
   192	        return output, total
   193	    return value, 0
   194	
   195	
   196	def _message_contract(index: int, total: int, role: str) -> tuple[ContextSectionType, ContextSourceKind, ContextTrust]:
   197	    if index == 0 and role == "system":
   198	        return (
   199	            ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   200	            ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
   201	            ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   202	        )
   203	    if role == "tool":
   204	        return (
   205	            ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   206	            ContextSourceKind.IMMUTABLE_ARTIFACT,
   207	            ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   208	        )
   209	    if role == "assistant":
   210	        return (
   211	            ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   212	            ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   213	            ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   214	        )
   215	    if index == total - 1:
   216	        return (
   217	            ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   218	            ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   219	            ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   220	        )
   221	    return ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT, ContextSourceKind.GOAL, ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION
   222	
   223	
   224	def _make_envelope(
   225	    sections: list[ContextSection],
   226	    *,
   227	    policy_version: str,
   228	    model_id: str,
   229	    versions: ContextVersionBindings,
   230	) -> ContextEnvelope:
   231	    values = {
   232	        "schema_version": 1,
   233	        "policy_version": policy_version,
   234	        "model_id": model_id,
   235	        "versions": versions,
   236	        "sections": tuple(sections),
   237	    }
   238	    hash_material = {
   239	        **values,
   240	        "versions": versions.model_dump(mode="json"),
   241	        "sections": [section.model_dump(mode="json") for section in sections],
   242	    }
   243	    return ContextEnvelope(**values, content_hash=content_hash(hash_material))
   244	
   245	
   246	def fit_messages_with_receipt(
   247	    messages: list[dict[str, Any]],
   248	    budget_tokens: int,
   249	    *,
   250	    model_id: str,
   251	    harness_version: str,
   252	    policy_version: str = "context-shadow-v1",
   253	    memory_snapshot_version: str | None = None,
   254	    evaluator_version: str = "not-bound:shadow",
   255	    weight_snapshot_version: str | None = None,
   256	    evidence_snapshot_version: str = "not-bound:shadow",
   257	    candidate_version: str = "live-prompt:shadow",
   258	    parent_candidate_version: str | None = None,
   259	    model_portfolio_version: str = "not-bound:shadow",
   260	    project_id: str = "meta-harness",
   261	    tier: Tier = Tier.SMALL,
   262	    redaction_values: Iterable[str] = (),
   263	    tool_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]] | None = None,
   264	) -> ContextFitReceipt:
   265	    """Fit exactly as before and build a deterministic, redacted sidecar receipt."""
   266	    originals = [dict(message) for message in messages]
   267	    fitted = fit_messages(messages, budget_tokens)
   268	    fitted = [dict(message) for message in fitted]
   269	    redaction_tuple = tuple(sorted(
   270	        {value for value in redaction_values if value},
   271	        key=lambda value: (-len(value), value),
   272	    ))
   273	    redacted_messages: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   274	    sections: list[ContextSection] = []
   275	    receipts: list[CompressionReceipt] = []
   276	    entries: list[ContextManifestEntry] = []
   277	    redaction_count = 0
   278	    tool_schema_tokens = 0
   279	
   280	    contracts = [
   281	        _message_contract(index, len(fitted), str(message.get("role") or "unknown"))
   282	        for index, message in enumerate(fitted)
   283	    ]
   284	    if tool_schemas:
   285	        contracts.append(
   286	            (
   287	                ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS,
   288	                ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   289	                ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   290	            )
   291	        )
   292	    section_budgets = allocate_section_budgets(
   293	        [contract[0] for contract in contracts], budget_tokens, tier
   294	    )
   295	
   296	    for index, (original, selected) in enumerate(zip(originals, fitted, strict=True)):
   297	        role = str(selected.get("role") or "unknown")
   298	        section_type, source_kind, trust = contracts[index]
   299	        original_content = str(original.get("content") or "")
   300	        selected_content = str(selected.get("content") or "")
   301	        before_hash, after_hash = content_hash(original_content), content_hash(selected_content)
   302	        action = CompressionAction.NONE if before_hash == after_hash else CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL
   303	        reason = "within allocated budget" if action is CompressionAction.NONE else "legacy deterministic budget fitting"
   304	        stable_id = f"message-{index:04d}-{role}"
   305	        source = ContextSourceRef(
   306	            source_id=stable_id,
   307	            kind=source_kind,
   308	            scope=ContextScope(project_id=project_id),
   309	            trust=trust,
   310	            content_hash=before_hash,
   311	            selection_reason="existing live prompt message observed in shadow mode",
   312	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   313	            fetchable=False,
   314	        )
   315	        original_tokens = estimate_tokens(original_content)
   316	        final_tokens = estimate_tokens(selected_content)
   317	        sections.append(
   318	            ContextSection(
   319	                section_type=section_type,
   320	                stable_id=stable_id,
   321	                source=source,
   322	                source_hash=before_hash,
   323	                trust=trust,
   324	                content=selected_content,
   325	                original_tokens=original_tokens,
   326	                selected_tokens=original_tokens,
   327	                compressed_tokens=final_tokens,
   328	                budget_tokens=section_budgets[index],
   329	                ordering_priority=index,
   330	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   331	                compression_action=action,
   332	                omission_reason=None if action is CompressionAction.NONE else reason,
   333	            )
   334	        )
   335	        receipts.append(
   336	            CompressionReceipt(
   337	                stable_id=stable_id,
   338	                action=action,
   339	                before_hash=before_hash,
   340	                after_hash=after_hash,
   341	                original_tokens=original_tokens,
   342	                final_tokens=final_tokens,
   343	                reason=reason,
   344	            )
   345	        )
   346	        redacted_message, count = _redact(selected, redaction_tuple)
   347	        redaction_count += count
   348	        redacted_messages.append(redacted_message)
   349	        entries.append(
   350	            ContextManifestEntry(
   351	                stable_id=stable_id,
   352	                surface="message",
   353	                payload_json=canonical_json(redacted_message),
   354	                source_kind=source_kind,
   355	                trust=trust,
   356	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   357	                source_hash=before_hash,
   358	                selected_hash=content_hash(redacted_message),
   359	                redacted=count > 0,
   360	            )
   361	        )
   362	
   363	    if tool_schemas:
   364	        stable_id = "tool-schemas"
   365	        schema_payload = [dict(schema) for schema in tool_schemas]
   366	        schema_hash = content_hash(schema_payload)
   367	        redacted_schemas, count = _redact(schema_payload, redaction_tuple)
   368	        redaction_count += count
   369	        source = ContextSourceRef(
   370	            source_id=stable_id,
   371	            kind=ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   372	            scope=ContextScope(project_id=project_id),
   373	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   374	            content_hash=schema_hash,
   375	            selection_reason="minimum task-authorized tool schemas observed in shadow mode",
   376	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   377	            fetchable=False,
   378	        )
   379	        schema_tokens = estimate_tokens(canonical_json(schema_payload))
   380	        tool_schema_tokens = schema_tokens
   381	        sections.append(
   382	            ContextSection(
   383	                section_type=ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS,
   384	                stable_id=stable_id,
   385	                source=source,
   386	                source_hash=schema_hash,
   387	                trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   388	                content=canonical_json(schema_payload),
   389	                original_tokens=schema_tokens,
   390	                selected_tokens=schema_tokens,
   391	                compressed_tokens=schema_tokens,
   392	                budget_tokens=section_budgets[-1],
   393	                ordering_priority=len(sections),
   394	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   395	            )
   396	        )
   397	        receipts.append(
   398	            CompressionReceipt(
   399	                stable_id=stable_id,
   400	                action=CompressionAction.NONE,
   401	                before_hash=schema_hash,
   402	                after_hash=schema_hash,
   403	                original_tokens=schema_tokens,
   404	                final_tokens=schema_tokens,
   405	                reason="within allocated budget",
   406	            )
   407	        )
   408	        entries.append(
   409	            ContextManifestEntry(
   410	                stable_id=stable_id,
   411	                surface="tool_schemas",
   412	                payload_json=canonical_json(redacted_schemas),
   413	                source_kind=ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   414	                trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   415	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   416	                source_hash=schema_hash,
   417	                selected_hash=content_hash(redacted_schemas),
   418	                redacted=count > 0,
   419	            )
   420	        )
   421	
   422	    versions = ContextVersionBindings(
   423	        model_portfolio_version=model_portfolio_version,
   424	        harness_version=harness_version,
   425	        evaluator_version=evaluator_version,
   426	        weight_snapshot_version=weight_snapshot_version,
   427	        memory_snapshot_version=memory_snapshot_version,
   428	        evidence_snapshot_version=evidence_snapshot_version,
   429	        candidate_version=candidate_version,
   430	        parent_candidate_version=parent_candidate_version,
     1	"""Typed, deterministic context contracts with legacy fitting compatibility."""

   228	class ContextEnvelope(FrozenModel):
   229	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   230	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   231	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   232	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   233	    sections: tuple[ContextSection, ...]
   234	    content_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   235	
   236	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   237	    def validate_hash_and_order(self) -> "ContextEnvelope":
   238	        if len({section.stable_id for section in self.sections}) != len(self.sections):
   239	            raise ValueError("section stable_id values must be unique")
   240	        priorities = [section.ordering_priority for section in self.sections]
   241	        if priorities != list(range(len(self.sections))):
   242	            raise ValueError("sections must have unique contiguous priorities")
   243	        project_ids = {section.source.scope.project_id for section in self.sections}
   244	        if len(project_ids) > 1:
   245	            raise ValueError(
   246	                "envelope sections must share a single source scope "
   247	                "project_id (no cross-project scope bleed); got "
   248	                f"{sorted(project_ids)}"
   249	            )
   250	        identity_by_source_id: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
   251	        for section in self.sections:
   252	            mode = "pinned" if section.source.content_hash is not None else "live"
   253	            identity_by_source_id.setdefault(section.source.source_id, set()).add(mode)
   254	        for source_id, modes in identity_by_source_id.items():
   255	            if len(modes) > 1:
   256	                raise ValueError(
   257	                    f"envelope sections sharing source_id={source_id!r} mix "
   258	                    "pinned (content_hash) and live (high_water_mark) identity "
   259	                    "without an explicit reconciliation marker (future "
   260	                    "marker: not yet supported)"
   261	                )
   262	        material = self.model_dump(mode="json", exclude={"content_hash"})
   263	        if self.content_hash != content_hash(material):
   264	            raise ValueError("envelope content_hash mismatch")
   265	        return self

   268	class CompressionReceipt(FrozenModel):
   269	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   270	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   271	    action: CompressionAction
   272	    before_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   273	    after_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   274	    original_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   275	    final_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   276	    reason: str = Field(min_length=1)
   277	    fidelity_loss_estimate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
   278	
   279	    @model_validator(mode="before")
   280	    @classmethod
   281	    def _fill_fidelity_loss_estimate(cls, data: Any) -> Any:
   282	        if not isinstance(data, dict) or "fidelity_loss_estimate" in data:
   283	            return data
   284	        action = data.get("action")
   285	        original = data.get("original_tokens") or 0
   286	        final = data.get("final_tokens") or 0
   287	        if action is CompressionAction.NONE:
   288	            data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = 0.0
   289	            return data
   290	        if original <= 0:
   291	            data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = 0.0 if final <= 0 else 1.0
   292	            return data
   293	        loss = 1.0 - (final / original)
   294	        if loss < 0.0:
   295	            loss = 0.0
   296	        elif loss > 1.0:
   297	            loss = 1.0
   298	        data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = loss
   299	        return data
   300	
   301	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   302	    def validate_change(self) -> "CompressionReceipt":
   303	        changed = self.before_hash != self.after_hash
   304	        if (self.action is CompressionAction.NONE) == changed:
   305	            raise ValueError("compression action must agree with before/after hashes")
   306	        return self
   307	
   308	
   309	class ContextManifestEntry(FrozenModel):
   310	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   311	    surface: Literal["message", "tool_schemas"]
   312	    payload_json: str = Field(min_length=2)
   313	    source_kind: ContextSourceKind
   314	    trust: ContextTrust
   315	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   316	    source_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   317	    selected_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   318	    redacted: bool = False
   319	
   320	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   321	    def validate_payload(self) -> "ContextManifestEntry":
   322	        try:
   323	            payload = json.loads(self.payload_json)
   324	        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
   325	            raise ValueError("payload_json must be canonical JSON") from exc
   326	        if self.payload_json != canonical_json(payload):
   327	            raise ValueError("payload_json must be canonical JSON")
   328	        if self.surface == "message" and not isinstance(payload, dict):
   329	            raise ValueError("message payload must be an object")
   330	        if self.surface == "tool_schemas" and not (
   331	            isinstance(payload, list) and all(isinstance(item, dict) for item in payload)
   332	        ):
   333	            raise ValueError("tool_schemas payload must be an object array")
   334	        if self.selected_hash != content_hash(payload):
   335	            raise ValueError("selected_hash must attest payload_json")
   336	        return self
   337	
   338	
   339	class ContextManifest(FrozenModel):
   340	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   341	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   342	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   343	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   344	    envelope_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   345	    redacted_envelope_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   346	    redacted_envelope_json: str = Field(min_length=2)
   347	    entries: tuple[ContextManifestEntry, ...]
   348	    compression_receipts: tuple[CompressionReceipt, ...]
   349	    source_candidates_considered: tuple[str, ...]
   350	    visibility_decisions: tuple[str, ...]
   351	    deliberate_omissions: tuple[str, ...]
   352	    artifact_refs: tuple[str, ...]
   353	    budget_used_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   354	    budget_limit_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   355	    redaction_count: int = Field(ge=0)
   356	    manifest_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   357	
   358	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   359	    def validate_manifest_hash(self) -> "ContextManifest":
   360	        if len(self.entries) != len(self.compression_receipts):
   361	            raise ValueError("each manifest entry requires a compression receipt")
   362	        if len({entry.stable_id for entry in self.entries}) != len(self.entries):
   363	            raise ValueError("manifest entry stable_id values must be unique")
   364	        if tuple(entry.stable_id for entry in self.entries) != tuple(
   365	            receipt.stable_id for receipt in self.compression_receipts
   366	        ):
   367	            raise ValueError("manifest entries and compression receipts must align")
   368	        material = self.model_dump(mode="json", exclude={"manifest_hash"})
   369	        if self.manifest_hash != content_hash(material):
   370	            raise ValueError("manifest_hash mismatch")
   371	        try:
   372	            redacted_envelope = json.loads(self.redacted_envelope_json)
   373	        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
   374	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_json must be canonical JSON") from exc
   375	        if self.redacted_envelope_json != canonical_json(redacted_envelope):
   376	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_json must be canonical JSON")
   377	        if self.redacted_envelope_hash != content_hash(redacted_envelope):
   378	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_hash mismatch")
   379	        envelope = ContextEnvelope.model_validate(redacted_envelope)
   380	        if envelope.content_hash != redacted_envelope.get("content_hash"):
   381	            raise ValueError("redacted envelope content hash mismatch")
   382	        required_artifact_refs = {
   383	            section.source.artifact_ref
   384	            for section in envelope.sections
   385	            if section.source.fetchable and section.source.artifact_ref is not None
   386	        }
   387	        provided_artifact_refs = set(self.artifact_refs)
   388	        missing = required_artifact_refs - provided_artifact_refs
   389	        if missing:
   390	            raise ValueError(
   391	                "artifact_refs must include every fetchable source's "
   392	                f"artifact_ref; missing: {sorted(missing)}"
   393	            )
   394	        return self
   395	
   396	    def reconstruct_messages(self) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   397	        return [json.loads(entry.payload_json) for entry in self.entries if entry.surface == "message"]
   398	
   399	    def reconstruct_tool_schemas(self) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   400	        schemas = [json.loads(entry.payload_json) for entry in self.entries if entry.surface == "tool_schemas"]
   401	        return [schema for group in schemas for schema in group]
   402	
   403	    def reconstruct_redacted_envelope(self) -> ContextEnvelope:
   404	        return ContextEnvelope.model_validate_json(self.redacted_envelope_json)

    29	TIER_CONTEXT_BUDGET: dict[Tier, int] = {
    30	    Tier.SMALL: 8_000,
    31	    Tier.MID: 16_000,
    32	    Tier.FRONTIER: 32_000,
    33	}
    34	GENERATION_RESERVE = 0.25
    35	
    36	TIER_SECTION_WEIGHTS: dict[Tier, dict[ContextSectionType, int]] = {
    37	    Tier.SMALL: {
    38	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS: 24,
    39	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT: 24,
    40	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS: 8,
    41	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    42	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 10,
    43	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 7,
    44	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 4,
    45	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 8,
    46	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 5,
    47	    },
    48	    Tier.MID: {
    49	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS: 20,
    50	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT: 21,
    51	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS: 9,
    52	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    53	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 14,
    54	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 9,
    55	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 5,
    56	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 7,
    57	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 5,
    58	    },
    59	    Tier.FRONTIER: {
    60	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS: 16,
    61	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT: 18,
    62	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS: 10,
    63	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    64	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 18,
    65	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 11,
    66	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 7,
    67	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 6,
    68	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 4,
    69	    },
    70	}
