    72	
    73	def estimate_tokens(text: str) -> int:
    74	    return len(text) // 4 + 1
    75	
    76	
    77	def messages_tokens(messages: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> int:
    78	    return sum(estimate_tokens(str(message.get("content") or "")) for message in messages)
    79	
    80	
    81	def budget_for(tier: Tier, override: int | None = None) -> int:
    82	    budget = override or TIER_CONTEXT_BUDGET.get(tier, 8_000)
    83	    return int(budget * (1 - GENERATION_RESERVE))
    84	
    85	
    86	def allocate_section_budgets(
    87	    section_types: list[ContextSectionType],
    88	    budget_tokens: int,
    89	    tier: Tier,
    90	) -> list[int]:
    91	    """Allocate the whole budget by tier using deterministic largest remainder."""
    92	    if budget_tokens < 0:
    93	        raise ValueError("budget_tokens must be nonnegative")
    94	    if not section_types:
    95	        return []
    96	    weights = TIER_SECTION_WEIGHTS[tier]
    97	    raw_weights = [weights[section_type] for section_type in section_types]
    98	    total_weight = sum(raw_weights)
    99	    numerators = [budget_tokens * weight for weight in raw_weights]
   100	    allocations = [numerator // total_weight for numerator in numerators]
   101	    remaining = budget_tokens - sum(allocations)
   102	    order = sorted(
   103	        range(len(section_types)),
   104	        key=lambda index: (-(numerators[index] % total_weight), index),
   105	    )
   106	    for index in order[:remaining]:
   107	        allocations[index] += 1
   108	    return allocations
   109	
   110	
   111	def fit_messages(messages: list[dict[str, Any]], budget_tokens: int) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   112	    """Preserve the pre-contract fitting behavior exactly for existing callers."""
   113	    if messages_tokens(messages) <= budget_tokens:
   114	        return messages
   115	    result = [dict(message) for message in messages]
   116	    prunable = [
   117	        index
   118	        for index, message in enumerate(result)
   119	        if not (index == 0 and message.get("role") == "system")
   120	        and index != len(result) - 1
   121	    ]
   122	
   123	    def priority(index: int) -> tuple[int, int]:
   124	        role_rank = 0 if result[index].get("role") == "tool" else 1
   125	        return role_rank, -len(str(result[index].get("content") or ""))
   126	
   127	    for index in sorted(prunable, key=priority):
   128	        if messages_tokens(result) <= budget_tokens:
   129	            break
   130	        text = str(result[index].get("content") or "")
   131	        overshoot = messages_tokens(result) - budget_tokens
   132	        target_chars = max(400, len(text) - overshoot * 4 - 200)
   133	        if target_chars < len(text):
   134	            result[index]["content"] = digest_text(text, target_chars)
   135	    return result
   136	
   137	
   138	class ContextFitReceipt(BaseModel):
   139	    """Internal sidecar: live messages plus the safe durable shadow receipt."""
   140	
   141	    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid", frozen=True)
   142	    messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   143	    redacted_messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   144	    envelope: ContextEnvelope
   145	    manifest: ContextManifest
   146	
   147	
   148	_BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS = (
   149	    re.compile(r"\bsk-[A-Za-z0-9_-]{8,}\b"),
   150	    re.compile(r"(?i)(authorization\s*:\s*bearer\s+)[^\s,;]+"),
   151	)
   152	
   153	
   154	def _redact_string(value: str, redaction_values: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[str, int]:
   155	    redacted = value
   156	    count = 0
   157	    for secret in redaction_values:
   158	        occurrences = redacted.count(secret)
   159	        if occurrences:
   160	            redacted = redacted.replace(secret, "[REDACTED]")
   161	            count += occurrences
   162	    for pattern in _BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS:
   163	        def replace(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
   164	            nonlocal count
   165	            count += 1
   166	            prefix = match.group(1) if match.lastindex else ""
   167	            return prefix + "[REDACTED]"
   168	
   169	        redacted = pattern.sub(replace, redacted)
   170	    return redacted, count
   171	
   172	
   173	def _redact(value: Any, redaction_values: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[Any, int]:
   174	    if isinstance(value, str):
   175	        return _redact_string(value, redaction_values)
   176	    if isinstance(value, list):
   177	        output, total = [], 0
   178	        for item in value:
   179	            clean, count = _redact(item, redaction_values)
   180	            output.append(clean)
   181	            total += count
   182	        return output, total
   183	    if isinstance(value, dict):
   184	        output, total = {}, 0
   185	        for key in sorted(value):
   186	            clean_key, key_count = _redact_string(key, redaction_values)
   187	            if clean_key != key:
   188	                clean_key = f"[REDACTED_KEY_{len(output)}]"
   189	            clean, count = _redact(value[key], redaction_values)
   190	            output[clean_key] = clean
   191	            total += key_count + count
   192	        return output, total
   193	    return value, 0
   194	
   195	
   196	def _message_contract(index: int, total: int, role: str) -> tuple[ContextSectionType, ContextSourceKind, ContextTrust]:
   197	    if index == 0 and role == "system":
   198	        return (
   199	            ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   200	            ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
   201	            ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   202	        )
   203	    if role == "tool":
   204	        return (
   205	            ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   206	            ContextSourceKind.IMMUTABLE_ARTIFACT,
   207	            ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   208	        )
   209	    if role == "assistant":
   210	        return (
   211	            ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   212	            ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   213	            ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   214	        )
   215	    if index == total - 1:
   216	        return (
   217	            ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   218	            ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   219	            ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   220	        )
   221	    return ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT, ContextSourceKind.GOAL, ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION
   222	
   223	
   224	def _make_envelope(
   225	    sections: list[ContextSection],
   226	    *,
   227	    policy_version: str,
   228	    model_id: str,
   229	    versions: ContextVersionBindings,
   230	) -> ContextEnvelope:
   231	    values = {
   232	        "schema_version": 1,
   233	        "policy_version": policy_version,
   234	        "model_id": model_id,
   235	        "versions": versions,
   236	        "sections": tuple(sections),
   237	    }
   238	    hash_material = {
   239	        **values,
   240	        "versions": versions.model_dump(mode="json"),
   241	        "sections": [section.model_dump(mode="json") for section in sections],
   242	    }
   243	    return ContextEnvelope(**values, content_hash=content_hash(hash_material))
   244	
   245	
   246	def fit_messages_with_receipt(
   247	    messages: list[dict[str, Any]],
   248	    budget_tokens: int,
   249	    *,
   250	    model_id: str,
   251	    harness_version: str,
   252	    policy_version: str = "context-shadow-v1",
   253	    memory_snapshot_version: str | None = None,
   254	    evaluator_version: str = "not-bound:shadow",
   255	    weight_snapshot_version: str | None = None,
   256	    evidence_snapshot_version: str = "not-bound:shadow",
   257	    candidate_version: str = "live-prompt:shadow",
   258	    parent_candidate_version: str | None = None,
   259	    model_portfolio_version: str = "not-bound:shadow",
   260	    project_id: str = "meta-harness",
   261	    tier: Tier = Tier.SMALL,
   262	    redaction_values: Iterable[str] = (),
   263	    tool_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]] | None = None,
   264	) -> ContextFitReceipt:
   265	    """Fit exactly as before and build a deterministic, redacted sidecar receipt."""
   266	    originals = [dict(message) for message in messages]
   267	    fitted = fit_messages(messages, budget_tokens)
   268	    fitted = [dict(message) for message in fitted]
   269	    redaction_tuple = tuple(sorted(
   270	        {value for value in redaction_values if value},
   271	        key=lambda value: (-len(value), value),
   272	    ))
   273	    redacted_messages: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   274	    sections: list[ContextSection] = []
   275	    receipts: list[CompressionReceipt] = []
   276	    entries: list[ContextManifestEntry] = []
   277	    redaction_count = 0
   278	    tool_schema_tokens = 0
   279	
   280	    contracts = [
   281	        _message_contract(index, len(fitted), str(message.get("role") or "unknown"))
   282	        for index, message in enumerate(fitted)
   283	    ]
   284	    if tool_schemas:
   285	        contracts.append(
   286	            (
   287	                ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS,
   288	                ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   289	                ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   290	            )
   291	        )
   292	    section_budgets = allocate_section_budgets(
   293	        [contract[0] for contract in contracts], budget_tokens, tier
   294	    )
   295	
   296	    for index, (original, selected) in enumerate(zip(originals, fitted, strict=True)):
   297	        role = str(selected.get("role") or "unknown")
   298	        section_type, source_kind, trust = contracts[index]
   299	        original_content = str(original.get("content") or "")
   300	        selected_content = str(selected.get("content") or "")
   301	        before_hash, after_hash = content_hash(original_content), content_hash(selected_content)
   302	        action = CompressionAction.NONE if before_hash == after_hash else CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL
   303	        reason = "within allocated budget" if action is CompressionAction.NONE else "legacy deterministic budget fitting"
   304	        stable_id = f"message-{index:04d}-{role}"
   305	        source = ContextSourceRef(
   306	            source_id=stable_id,
   307	            kind=source_kind,
   308	            scope=ContextScope(project_id=project_id),
   309	            trust=trust,
   310	            content_hash=before_hash,
   311	            selection_reason="existing live prompt message observed in shadow mode",
   312	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   313	            fetchable=False,
   314	        )
   315	        original_tokens = estimate_tokens(original_content)
   316	        final_tokens = estimate_tokens(selected_content)
   317	        sections.append(
   318	            ContextSection(
   319	                section_type=section_type,
   320	                stable_id=stable_id,
   321	                source=source,
   322	                source_hash=before_hash,
   323	                trust=trust,
   324	                content=selected_content,
   325	                original_tokens=original_tokens,
   326	                selected_tokens=original_tokens,
   327	                compressed_tokens=final_tokens,
   328	                budget_tokens=section_budgets[index],
   329	                ordering_priority=index,
   330	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   331	                compression_action=action,
   332	                omission_reason=None if action is CompressionAction.NONE else reason,
   333	            )
   334	        )
   335	        receipts.append(
   336	            CompressionReceipt(
   337	                stable_id=stable_id,
   338	                action=action,
   339	                before_hash=before_hash,
   340	                after_hash=after_hash,
   341	                original_tokens=original_tokens,
   342	                final_tokens=final_tokens,
   343	                reason=reason,
   344	            )
   345	        )
   346	        redacted_message, count = _redact(selected, redaction_tuple)
   347	        redaction_count += count
   348	        redacted_messages.append(redacted_message)
   349	        entries.append(
   350	            ContextManifestEntry(
   351	                stable_id=stable_id,
   352	                surface="message",
   353	                payload_json=canonical_json(redacted_message),
   354	                source_kind=source_kind,
   355	                trust=trust,
   356	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   357	                source_hash=before_hash,
   358	                selected_hash=content_hash(redacted_message),
   359	                redacted=count > 0,
   360	            )
   361	        )
   362	
   363	    if tool_schemas:
   364	        stable_id = "tool-schemas"
   365	        schema_payload = [dict(schema) for schema in tool_schemas]
   366	        schema_hash = content_hash(schema_payload)
   367	        redacted_schemas, count = _redact(schema_payload, redaction_tuple)
   368	        redaction_count += count
   369	        source = ContextSourceRef(
   370	            source_id=stable_id,
   371	            kind=ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   372	            scope=ContextScope(project_id=project_id),
   373	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   374	            content_hash=schema_hash,
   375	            selection_reason="minimum task-authorized tool schemas observed in shadow mode",
   376	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   377	            fetchable=False,
   378	        )
   379	        schema_tokens = estimate_tokens(canonical_json(schema_payload))
   380	        tool_schema_tokens = schema_tokens
   381	        sections.append(
   382	            ContextSection(
   383	                section_type=ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS,
   384	                stable_id=stable_id,
   385	                source=source,
   386	                source_hash=schema_hash,
   387	                trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   388	                content=canonical_json(schema_payload),
   389	                original_tokens=schema_tokens,
   390	                selected_tokens=schema_tokens,
   391	                compressed_tokens=schema_tokens,
   392	                budget_tokens=section_budgets[-1],
   393	                ordering_priority=len(sections),
   394	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   395	            )
   396	        )
   397	        receipts.append(
   398	            CompressionReceipt(
   399	                stable_id=stable_id,
   400	                action=CompressionAction.NONE,
   401	                before_hash=schema_hash,
   402	                after_hash=schema_hash,
   403	                original_tokens=schema_tokens,
   404	                final_tokens=schema_tokens,
   405	                reason="within allocated budget",
   406	            )
   407	        )
   408	        entries.append(
   409	            ContextManifestEntry(
   410	                stable_id=stable_id,
   411	                surface="tool_schemas",
   412	                payload_json=canonical_json(redacted_schemas),
   413	                source_kind=ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   414	                trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   415	                sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   416	                source_hash=schema_hash,
   417	                selected_hash=content_hash(redacted_schemas),
   418	                redacted=count > 0,
   419	            )
   420	        )
   421	
   422	    versions = ContextVersionBindings(
   423	        model_portfolio_version=model_portfolio_version,
   424	        harness_version=harness_version,
   425	        evaluator_version=evaluator_version,
   426	        weight_snapshot_version=weight_snapshot_version,
   427	        memory_snapshot_version=memory_snapshot_version,
   428	        evidence_snapshot_version=evidence_snapshot_version,
   429	        candidate_version=candidate_version,
   430	        parent_candidate_version=parent_candidate_version,
   431	    )
   432	    envelope = _make_envelope(
   433	        sections,
   434	        policy_version=policy_version,
   435	        model_id=model_id,
   436	        versions=versions,
   437	    )
   438	    redacted_envelope, _ = _redact(envelope.model_dump(mode="json"), redaction_tuple)
   439	    redacted_envelope_material = {
   440	        key: value for key, value in redacted_envelope.items() if key != "content_hash"
   441	    }
   442	    redacted_envelope["content_hash"] = content_hash(redacted_envelope_material)
   443	    redacted_envelope_json = canonical_json(redacted_envelope)
   444	    manifest_values = {
   445	        "schema_version": 1,
   446	        "policy_version": policy_version,
   447	        "model_id": model_id,
   448	        "versions": versions,
   449	        "envelope_hash": envelope.content_hash,
   450	        "redacted_envelope_hash": content_hash(redacted_envelope),
   451	        "redacted_envelope_json": redacted_envelope_json,
   452	        "entries": tuple(entries),
   453	        "compression_receipts": tuple(receipts),
   454	        "source_candidates_considered": tuple(entry.stable_id for entry in entries),
   455	        "visibility_decisions": tuple(f"{entry.stable_id}:included" for entry in entries),
   456	        "deliberate_omissions": (),
   457	        "artifact_refs": (),
   458	        "budget_used_tokens": messages_tokens(fitted) + tool_schema_tokens,
   459	        "budget_limit_tokens": budget_tokens,
   460	        "redaction_count": redaction_count,
   461	    }
   462	    serializable = {
   463	        **manifest_values,
   464	        "versions": versions.model_dump(mode="json"),
   465	        "entries": [entry.model_dump(mode="json") for entry in entries],
   466	        "compression_receipts": [receipt.model_dump(mode="json") for receipt in receipts],
   467	    }
   468	    manifest = ContextManifest(
   469	        **manifest_values,
   470	        manifest_hash=content_hash(serializable),
   471	    )
   472	    return ContextFitReceipt(
   473	        messages=fitted,
   474	        redacted_messages=redacted_messages,
   475	        envelope=envelope,
   476	        manifest=manifest,
   477	    )

     1	"""OpenAI-compatible endpoint worker — first-class support for local on-device
     2	models (Ollama, LM Studio, vLLM, MLX servers).
     3	
     4	Motivation: OPD-distilled small models (MiniCPM5-1B class) now punch far above
     5	their size on the domains their RL teachers covered. The SMALL tier therefore
     6	can't assume "cloud API" — a 1B model on the user's own machine is a legitimate
     7	worker. Anything speaking the OpenAI chat-completions dialect plugs in here.
     8	
     9	Notes for hybrid-thinking models (MiniCPM5, Qwen3.x): pass
    10	`thinking=True/False` and it is forwarded as `chat_template_kwargs.enable_thinking`
    11	(the vLLM/SGLang convention) — the router can buy accuracy with latency per task.
    12	"""
    13	from __future__ import annotations
    14	
    15	import json
    16	import re
    17	from typing import Any, Optional
    18	
    19	import httpx
    20	
    21	from metaharness.core.types import Task, Tier, WorkerResult
    22	from metaharness.harness.runner import BaseRunner, WorkerTimeout
    23	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    24	from metaharness.observability.run_events import emit_run_event
    25	
    26	
    27	async def probe_endpoint(base_url: str, timeout_s: float = 3.0,
    28	                         api_key: str = "") -> Optional[list[str]]:
    29	    """Return the model ids served at an OpenAI-compatible base_url, or None if
    30	    unreachable. Use this before wiring a worker — never point at a guess."""
    31	    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
    32	    try:
    33	        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=timeout_s, headers=headers) as client:
    34	            resp = await client.get(f"{base_url.rstrip('/')}/models")
    35	            resp.raise_for_status()
    36	            return [m["id"] for m in resp.json().get("data", [])]
    37	    except (httpx.HTTPError, KeyError, ValueError):
    38	        return None
    39	
    40	
    41	def _build_messages(task: Task, system_prompt: str = "") -> list[dict[str, str]]:
    42	    """Render the Task's explicit delegation contract into chat messages."""
    43	    system_parts = [system_prompt or "You are a worker agent executing one well-scoped task."]
    44	    if task.boundaries:
    45	        system_parts.append("Boundaries:\n" + "\n".join(f"- {b}" for b in task.boundaries))
    46	    if task.output_schema:
    47	        system_parts.append(
    48	            "Respond with a single JSON object matching this schema exactly, "
    49	            "no prose around it:\n" + json.dumps(task.output_schema)
    50	        )
    51	    user_parts = [task.objective]
    52	    if task.inputs:
    53	        visible = {k: v for k, v in task.inputs.items() if not k.startswith("_")}
    54	        if visible:
    55	            user_parts.append("Inputs:\n" + json.dumps(visible, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
    56	    return [
    57	        {"role": "system", "content": "\n\n".join(system_parts)},
    58	        {"role": "user", "content": "\n\n".join(user_parts)},
    59	    ]
    60	
    61	
    62	_FENCE_RE = re.compile(r"```(?:json)?\s*(.*?)```", re.DOTALL)
    63	
    64	
    65	_THINK_RE = re.compile(r"<think>.*?</think>\s*", re.DOTALL)
    66	
    67	
    68	def strip_think(text: str) -> str:
    69	    """Drop <think>…</think> reasoning blocks that hybrid-thinking models
    70	    (MiniMax, Qwen3, DeepSeek-R1) emit inline before the answer — the answer
    71	    is what gets parsed and verified, never the deliberation. An UNCLOSED
    72	    block (max_tokens mid-thought) drops everything from the tag on: half a
    73	    thought must not masquerade as the answer.
    74	
    75	    Bug this guards against (2026-07-09): MiniMax-M3 answered every classify
    76	    task correctly after a think block, and the harness-tuning verifier
    77	    scored the whole suite pass^3=0.00 because raw text was compared against
    78	    the expected label."""
    79	    stripped = _THINK_RE.sub("", text)
    80	    if "<think>" in stripped:
    81	        stripped = stripped.split("<think>", 1)[0]
    82	    return stripped.strip()
    83	
    84	
    85	def parse_output(text: str, expect_json: bool) -> Any:
    86	    """Best-effort structured parse: fenced JSON, bare JSON, else raw text."""
    87	    if not expect_json:
    88	        return text
    89	    candidate = text.strip()
    90	    fence = _FENCE_RE.search(candidate)
    91	    if fence:
    92	        candidate = fence.group(1).strip()
    93	    try:
    94	        return json.loads(candidate)
    95	    except ValueError:
    96	        # last resort: first {...} block in the text
    97	        start, end = candidate.find("{"), candidate.rfind("}")
    98	        if 0 <= start < end:
    99	            try:
   100	                return json.loads(candidate[start : end + 1])
   101	            except ValueError:
   102	                pass
   103	        return text
   104	
   105	
   106	class OpenAICompatWorker(BaseRunner):
   107	    """A worker backed by any OpenAI-compatible /chat/completions endpoint."""
   108	
   109	    def __init__(
   110	        self,
   111	        worker_id: str,
   112	        base_url: str,
   113	        model: str,
   114	        tier: Tier = Tier.SMALL,
   115	        api_key: str = "",
   116	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   117	        temperature: float = 0.2,
   118	        max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
   119	        thinking: Optional[bool] = None,
   120	        extra_body: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
   121	        cost_per_1k_tokens: float = 0.0,  # local inference is free by default
   122	        timeout_s: float = 120.0,
   123	        system_prompt: str = "",  # persona/role prefix; task contract still appended
   124	        tool_registry=None,        # ToolRegistry; wired by HarnessState.wire()
   125	        context_budget: Optional[int] = None,  # tokens; default by tier
   126	        max_tool_rounds: int = 5,
   127	        client: Optional[httpx.AsyncClient] = None,  # injectable for tests
   128	    ) -> None:
   129	        super().__init__(worker_id=worker_id, tier=tier, model=model, keypair=keypair)
   130	        self.base_url = base_url.rstrip("/")
   131	        self.api_key = api_key
   132	        self.system_prompt = system_prompt
   133	        self.tool_registry = tool_registry
   134	        self.context_budget = context_budget
   135	        self.max_tool_rounds = max_tool_rounds
   136	        self.temperature = temperature
   137	        self.max_tokens = max_tokens
   138	        self.thinking = thinking
   139	        self.extra_body = extra_body or {}
   140	        self.cost_per_1k_tokens = cost_per_1k_tokens
   141	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s
   142	        self._client = client
   143	
   144	    def _tool_schemas(self, task: Task) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   145	        if not task.tools or self.tool_registry is None:
   146	            return []
   147	        return self.tool_registry.openai_schemas(task.tools)
   148	
   149	    def _body(self, task: Task, messages: list[dict[str, Any]],
   150	              tool_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   151	        body: dict[str, Any] = {
   152	            "model": self.model,
   153	            "messages": messages,
   154	            "temperature": self.temperature,
   155	        }
   156	        if self.max_tokens is not None:
   157	            body["max_tokens"] = self.max_tokens
   158	        if tool_schemas:
   159	            body["tools"] = tool_schemas
   160	        if task.output_schema:
   161	            body["response_format"] = {"type": "json_object"}
   162	        if self.thinking is not None:
   163	            body["chat_template_kwargs"] = {"enable_thinking": self.thinking}
   164	        body.update(self.extra_body)
   165	        return body
   166	
   167	    async def _post(self, client: httpx.AsyncClient, body: dict[str, Any],
   168	                    headers: dict[str, str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   169	        resp = await client.post(
   170	            f"{self.base_url}/chat/completions", json=body, headers=headers
   171	        )
   172	        if resp.status_code == 400 and "response_format" in body:
   173	            # servers disagree on structured-output dialects (LM Studio wants
   174	            # json_schema, Ollama takes json_object) — the prompt already
   175	            # demands JSON, so retry bare rather than fail the attempt
   176	            body.pop("response_format")
   177	            resp = await client.post(
   178	                f"{self.base_url}/chat/completions", json=body, headers=headers
   179	            )
   180	        resp.raise_for_status()
   181	        return resp.json()
   182	
   183	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   184	        from metaharness.context import (
   185	            budget_for,
   186	            content_hash,
   187	            fit_messages_with_receipt,
   188	        )
   189	
   190	        headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
   191	        if self.api_key:
   192	            headers["Authorization"] = f"Bearer {self.api_key}"
   193	        messages = _build_messages(task, self.system_prompt)
   194	        tool_schemas = self._tool_schemas(task)
   195	        prompt_budget = budget_for(self.tier, self.context_budget)
   196	        tool_calls_made: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   197	        tokens_in = tokens_out = 0
   198	
   199	        client = self._client or httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=self.timeout_s)
   200	        try:
   201	            for _round in range(self.max_tool_rounds + 1):
   202	                unfitted_messages = messages
   203	                try:
   204	                    context_receipt = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   205	                        unfitted_messages,
   206	                        prompt_budget,
   207	                        model_id=self.model,
   208	                        harness_version="metaharness:0.1.0",
   209	                        tier=self.tier,
   210	                        tool_schemas=tool_schemas,
   211	                        redaction_values=[self.api_key] if self.api_key else (),
   212	                    )
   213	                except Exception as exc:
   214	                    # Shadow evidence must never alter the live prompt path.
   215	                    # Invalid direct contract inputs still fail closed at the
   216	                    # public model/assembler boundary; this runtime observer
   217	                    # falls back to the exact legacy fitter.
   218	                    from metaharness.context import fit_messages
   219	
   220	                    messages = fit_messages(unfitted_messages, prompt_budget)
   221	                    try:
   222	                        emit_run_event(
   223	                            "context.manifest.shadow_failed",
   224	                            {
   225	                                "schema_version": 1,
   226	                                "shadow": True,
   227	                                "task_id": task.id,
   228	                                "error_type": type(exc).__name__,
   229	                            },
   230	                        )
   231	                    except Exception:
   232	                        pass
   233	                else:
   234	                    messages = context_receipt.messages
   235	                    try:
   236	                        emit_run_event(
   237	                            "context.manifest.shadow",
   238	                            {
   239	                                "schema_version": 1,
   240	                                "shadow": True,
   241	                                "task_id": task.id,
   242	                                "live_messages_hash": content_hash(messages),
   243	                                "manifest": context_receipt.manifest.model_dump(mode="json"),
   244	                            },
   245	                        )
   246	                    except Exception:
   247	                        # A telemetry sink is outside candidate execution
   248	                        # authority and cannot make the model call fail.
   249	                        pass
   250	                try:
   251	                    data = await self._post(
   252	                        client, self._body(task, messages, tool_schemas), headers)
   253	                except httpx.TimeoutException as exc:
   254	                    # parity with CodingAgentWorker (issue #2): without this, a
   255	                    # config-exposed openai_compat timeout would journal as
   256	                    # timed_out=False / tool_error — a contract lie. Wraps ONLY
   257	                    # the model call: an httpx timeout escaping a tool handler
   258	                    # is a tool error, not a model timeout (issue #2 panel,
   259	                    # Claude+codex P2). :g not :.0f — subsecond test timeouts
   260	                    # must not render as "0s".
   261	                    raise WorkerTimeout(
   262	                        f"openai_compat: timed out after {self.timeout_s:g}s",
   263	                        timeout_s=self.timeout_s,
   264	                    ) from exc
   265	                usage = data.get("usage") or {}
   266	                tokens_in += int(usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0))
   267	                tokens_out += int(usage.get("completion_tokens", 0))
   268	                message = data["choices"][0]["message"]
   269	                calls = message.get("tool_calls") or []
   270	                if not calls or not tool_schemas or _round == self.max_tool_rounds:
   271	                    break
   272	                # tool round: run each call, feed pruned observations back
   273	                messages.append({"role": "assistant", "content": message.get("content"),
   274	                                 "tool_calls": calls})
   275	                for call in calls:
   276	                    fn = call.get("function") or {}
   277	                    name = fn.get("name", "")
   278	                    try:
   279	                        arguments = json.loads(fn.get("arguments") or "{}")
   280	                    except ValueError:
   281	                        arguments = {}
   282	                    observation = await self.tool_registry.call(
   283	                        name, arguments, focus=task.objective)
   284	                    tool_calls_made.append(
   285	                        {"tool": name, "arguments": arguments,
   286	                         "result_preview": observation[:200]})
   287	                    messages.append({"role": "tool",
   288	                                     "tool_call_id": call.get("id", name),
   289	                                     "content": observation})
   290	        finally:
   291	            if self._client is None:
   292	                await client.aclose()
   293	
   294	        text = strip_think(message.get("content") or "")
   295	        if not text and message.get("reasoning_content"):
   296	            # thinking model hit max_tokens mid-reasoning; surface what exists
   297	            text = message["reasoning_content"]
   298	        return WorkerResult(
   299	            task_id=task.id,
   300	            worker_id=self.worker_id,
   301	            tier=self.tier,
   302	            model=self.model,
   303	            output=parse_output(text, expect_json=bool(task.output_schema)),
   304	            raw_text=text,
   305	            tool_calls=tool_calls_made,
   306	            tokens_in=tokens_in,
   307	            tokens_out=tokens_out,
   308	            cost_usd=(tokens_in + tokens_out) / 1000 * self.cost_per_1k_tokens,
   309	            workspace_root=getattr(self.tool_registry, "workspace_root", "")
   310	            if self.tool_registry is not None else "",
   311	        )
     1	"""Coding-agent CLI workers: delegate CODE_EDIT-class tasks to a full coding
     2	harness (Pi, Codex CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code) running headless in a managed
     3	workspace.
     4	
     5	Motivation: these CLIs are complete agent harnesses — file editing, shell,
     6	search, their own verification loops. Wrapping one as a Runner gives the
     7	meta-harness hands: it can implement its own plans, generate experiment code,
     8	and produce artifacts the eval layer can grade. Per design principle "worker
     9	output is data": the CLI's stdout is parsed, never interpreted as instructions.
    10	
    11	Invocation recipes follow memory/knowledge_base/coding-agent-clis-mcp.md —
    12	one-shot headless, prompt over stdin where the CLI supports it (untrusted task
    13	text never lands in argv), session persistence off, cwd pinned to the
    14	workspace.
    15	"""
    16	from __future__ import annotations
    17	
    18	import asyncio
    19	import json
    20	import os
    21	import re
    22	import signal
    23	import shutil
    24	import sys
    25	import tempfile
    26	from dataclasses import dataclass
    27	from pathlib import Path
    28	from typing import Callable, Optional
    29	
    30	from metaharness.core.types import Task, TaskType, Tier, WorkerResult
    31	from metaharness.harness.runner import BaseRunner, WorkerTimeout
    32	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    33	from metaharness.routing.eligibility import child_host_environment
    34	
    35	WORKSPACES_DIR = Path.home() / ".metaharness" / "workspaces"
    36	
    37	# a coding CLI implementing a plan needs far more wall-clock than a one-shot
    38	# text task; scale the base timeout by task type (issue #2). Precedent for
    39	# table+override shape: context.TIER_CONTEXT_BUDGET / budget_for().
    40	TASK_TYPE_TIMEOUT_FACTOR: dict[TaskType, float] = {TaskType.CODE_EDIT: 3.0}
    41	
    42	
    43	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    44	class CLIAdapter:
    45	    """How to drive one coding CLI headless: argv builder + output parser."""
    46	
    47	    binary: str
    48	    build: Callable[["CodingAgentWorker", str, Path], tuple[list[str], Optional[str]]]
    49	    # build(worker, prompt, workspace) -> (argv, stdin_text or None)
    50	    parse: Callable[[str], tuple[str, float]]
    51	    # parse(stdout) -> (final_text, cost_usd)
    52	
    53	
    54	def _parse_text(stdout: str) -> tuple[str, float]:
    55	    return stdout.strip(), 0.0
    56	
    57	
    58	def _parse_claude_json(stdout: str) -> tuple[str, float]:
    59	    try:
    60	        data = json.loads(stdout)
    61	        return str(data.get("result", "")), float(data.get("total_cost_usd", 0.0))
    62	    except (ValueError, TypeError):
    63	        return stdout.strip(), 0.0
    64	
    65	
    66	def _parse_pi_jsonl(stdout: str) -> tuple[str, float]:
    67	    """Last assistant text across Pi's --mode json event stream."""
    68	    text, cost = "", 0.0
    69	    for line in stdout.splitlines():
    70	        try:
    71	            event = json.loads(line)
    72	        except ValueError:
    73	            continue
    74	        message = event.get("message") or {}
    75	        if message.get("role") == "assistant":
    76	            content = message.get("content")
    77	            if isinstance(content, list):
    78	                parts = [c.get("text", "") for c in content if isinstance(c, dict)]
    79	                text = "\n".join(p for p in parts if p) or text
    80	            elif isinstance(content, str) and content:
    81	                text = content
    82	        usage = event.get("usage") or message.get("usage") or {}
    83	        if isinstance(usage, dict):
    84	            cost = float(usage.get("cost", {}).get("total", cost)) if isinstance(usage.get("cost"), dict) else cost
    85	    return text or stdout.strip(), cost
    86	
    87	
    88	def _build_pi(worker: "CodingAgentWorker", prompt: str, ws: Path) -> tuple[list[str], Optional[str]]:
    89	    argv = [worker.binary, "--mode", "json", "--no-session", "--no-extensions",
    90	            "--no-skills", "--no-prompt-templates", "--no-themes"]
    91	    if worker.cli_model:
    92	        argv += ["--model", worker.cli_model]
    93	    if worker.system_prompt:
    94	        argv += ["--append-system-prompt", worker.system_prompt]
    95	    argv += ["-p"]
    96	    return argv, prompt
    97	
    98	
    99	def _build_codex(worker: "CodingAgentWorker", prompt: str, ws: Path) -> tuple[list[str], Optional[str]]:
   100	    sandbox = getattr(worker, "sandbox", "workspace-write")
   101	    argv = [worker.binary, "exec", "--skip-git-repo-check", "--sandbox", sandbox,
   102	            "--cd", str(ws)]
   103	    if sandbox == "read-only":
   104	        argv += ["--ephemeral"]
   105	    if worker.cli_model:
   106	        argv += ["-m", worker.cli_model]
   107	    argv += ["-"]  # prompt from stdin
   108	    return argv, prompt
   109	
   110	
   111	def _build_opencode(worker: "CodingAgentWorker", prompt: str, ws: Path) -> tuple[list[str], Optional[str]]:
   112	    argv = [worker.binary, "run"]
   113	    if worker.cli_model:
   114	        argv += ["-m", worker.cli_model]
   115	    argv += [prompt]
   116	    return argv, None
   117	
   118	
   119	def _build_claude(worker: "CodingAgentWorker", prompt: str, ws: Path) -> tuple[list[str], Optional[str]]:
   120	    argv = [worker.binary, "-p", "--output-format", "json"]
   121	    if getattr(worker, "sandbox", None) == "read-only":
   122	        argv += ["--safe-mode", "--no-session-persistence",
   123	                 "--permission-mode", "plan", "--tools", "Read,Glob,Grep"]
   124	    if worker.cli_model:
   125	        argv += ["--model", worker.cli_model]
   126	    if worker.system_prompt:
   127	        argv += ["--append-system-prompt", worker.system_prompt]
   128	    return argv, prompt
   129	
   130	
   131	CLI_ADAPTERS: dict[str, CLIAdapter] = {
   132	    "pi": CLIAdapter(binary="pi", build=_build_pi, parse=_parse_pi_jsonl),
   133	    "codex": CLIAdapter(binary="codex", build=_build_codex, parse=_parse_text),
   134	    "opencode": CLIAdapter(binary="opencode", build=_build_opencode, parse=_parse_text),
   135	    "claude": CLIAdapter(binary="claude", build=_build_claude, parse=_parse_claude_json),
   136	}
   137	
   138	
   139	def available_clis() -> dict[str, str]:
   140	    """Which coding CLIs are installed on this machine (name -> path)."""
   141	    found = {}
   142	    for name, adapter in CLI_ADAPTERS.items():
   143	        path = shutil.which(adapter.binary)
   144	        if path:
   145	            found[name] = path
   146	    return found
   147	
   148	
   149	# each coding harness authenticates ITSELF — the meta-harness never stores or
   150	# proxies these keys, it only tells the user where they live
   151	CLI_KEY_HINTS: dict[str, str] = {
   152	    "pi": "keys: standard env vars (ANTHROPIC_API_KEY, …) or ~/.pi/agent/auth.json",
   153	    "codex": "auth: `codex login` (ChatGPT OAuth) or CODEX_API_KEY; config in ~/.codex/config.toml",
   154	    "opencode": "keys: `opencode auth login` or provider.options.apiKey in ~/.config/opencode/opencode.json",
   155	    "claude": "auth: `claude login` (subscription) or ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
   156	}
   157	
   158	# CLIs that can enumerate their own models; others fall back to known aliases
   159	_CLI_MODEL_LISTERS: dict[str, list[str]] = {
   160	    "pi": ["--list-models"],
   161	    "opencode": ["models"],
   162	}
   163	_CLI_STATIC_MODELS: dict[str, list[str]] = {
   164	    "claude": ["sonnet", "opus", "haiku", "claude-fable-5", "claude-opus-4-8"],
   165	    "codex": ["gpt-5.2-codex", "gpt-5.2", "o5"],
   166	}
   167	
   168	_MODEL_ID_RE = re.compile(r"^[A-Za-z0-9][\w.\-]*(/[\w.\-:]+)+$")
   169	
   170	PI_MODELS_PATH = Path.home() / ".pi" / "agent" / "models.json"
   171	OPENCODE_CONFIG_PATHS = [
   172	    Path.home() / ".config" / "opencode" / "opencode.json",
   173	    Path.home() / ".config" / "opencode" / "opencode.jsonc",
   174	]
   175	
   176	
   177	def _load_jsonish(path: Path) -> dict:
   178	    """JSON, tolerating the JSONC subset opencode uses (full-line comments,
   179	    trailing commas). Anything unparseable yields {} — suggestions only."""
   180	    try:
   181	        text = path.read_text()
   182	    except OSError:
   183	        return {}
   184	    try:
   185	        return json.loads(text)
   186	    except ValueError:
   187	        stripped = "\n".join(
   188	            line for line in text.splitlines() if not line.lstrip().startswith("//")
   189	        )
   190	        stripped = re.sub(r",(\s*[}\]])", r"\1", stripped)
   191	        try:
   192	            return json.loads(stripped)
   193	        except ValueError:
   194	            return {}
   195	
   196	
   197	def pi_config_models(path: Path = PI_MODELS_PATH) -> list[str]:
   198	    """provider/model ids from Pi's custom model registry (~/.pi/agent/
   199	    models.json) — the ids Pi itself accepts via --model."""
   200	    data = _load_jsonish(path)
   201	    models = []
   202	    for pid, provider in (data.get("providers") or {}).items():
   203	        for entry in provider.get("models") or []:
   204	            if isinstance(entry, dict) and entry.get("id"):
   205	                models.append(f"{pid}/{entry['id']}")
   206	    return models
   207	
   208	
   209	def opencode_config_models(paths: Optional[list[Path]] = None) -> list[str]:
   210	    """provider/model ids from OpenCode's config (opencode.json[c])."""
   211	    models = []
   212	    for path in paths or OPENCODE_CONFIG_PATHS:
   213	        data = _load_jsonish(path)
   214	        for pid, provider in (data.get("provider") or {}).items():
   215	            if isinstance(provider, dict):
   216	                for mid in (provider.get("models") or {}):
   217	                    models.append(f"{pid}/{mid}")
   218	        if models:
   219	            break
   220	    return models
   221	
   222	
   223	_CLI_CONFIG_MODELS = {
   224	    "pi": pi_config_models,
   225	    "opencode": opencode_config_models,
   226	}
   227	
   228	
   229	async def list_cli_models(cli: str, timeout_s: float = 15.0,
   230	                          cap: int = 300) -> list[str]:
   231	    """The models a coding CLI can use, asked from the CLI itself when it
   232	    supports listing. Failures fall back to the static aliases — a model id
   233	    is a suggestion, not a gate; the CLI validates it at run time."""
   234	    if cli not in CLI_ADAPTERS:
   235	        raise ValueError(f"unknown coding CLI {cli!r}")
   236	    lister = _CLI_MODEL_LISTERS.get(cli)
   237	    # the CLI's own config directory is the fastest, most personal source:
   238	    # custom registries (pi models.json) and configured providers (opencode)
   239	    config_reader = _CLI_CONFIG_MODELS.get(cli)
   240	    configured = config_reader() if config_reader else []
   241	    static = _dedupe(configured + _CLI_STATIC_MODELS.get(cli, []))
   242	    binary = shutil.which(CLI_ADAPTERS[cli].binary)
   243	    if lister is None or binary is None:
   244	        return static
   245	    try:
   246	        proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
   247	            binary, *lister,
   248	            stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE, stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   249	            stdin=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   250	        )
   251	        stdout_b, _ = await asyncio.wait_for(proc.communicate(), timeout=timeout_s)
   252	    except (OSError, asyncio.TimeoutError):
   253	        try:
   254	            proc.kill()
   255	        except Exception:
   256	            pass
   257	        return static
   258	    models = []
   259	    for line in stdout_b.decode(errors="replace").splitlines():
   260	        token = line.strip().split()[0] if line.strip() else ""
   261	        if _MODEL_ID_RE.match(token):
   262	            models.append(token)
   263	            if len(models) >= cap:
   264	                break
   265	    return _dedupe(configured + models)[:cap] or static
   266	
   267	
   268	def _dedupe(items: list[str]) -> list[str]:
   269	    seen: set[str] = set()
   270	    return [x for x in items if not (x in seen or seen.add(x))]
   271	
   272	
   273	def _render_prompt(task: Task) -> str:
   274	    """The Task delegation contract as one prompt for a coding agent."""
   275	    parts = [task.objective]
   276	    if task.boundaries:
   277	        parts.append("Constraints:\n" + "\n".join(f"- {b}" for b in task.boundaries))
   278	    visible = {k: v for k, v in (task.inputs or {}).items() if not k.startswith("_")}
   279	    if visible:
   280	        parts.append("Inputs:\n" + json.dumps(visible, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
   281	    if task.output_schema:
   282	        parts.append(
   283	            "When done, print a final summary as a single JSON object matching:\n"
   284	            + json.dumps(task.output_schema)
   285	        )
   286	    return "\n\n".join(parts)
   287	
   288	
   289	class CodingAgentWorker(BaseRunner):
   290	    """A worker that runs a coding-agent CLI one-shot per task in a workspace.
   291	
   292	    Every run is headless and ephemeral (no CLI-side session state); the
   293	    workspace directory is the durable artifact. A non-zero exit or a spawn
   294	    failure becomes WorkerResult.error — loud, never a silent pass.
   295	    """
   296	
   297	    BASE_TIMEOUT_S: float = 600.0
   298	
   299	    def __init__(
   300	        self,
   301	        worker_id: str,
   302	        cli: str,
   303	        model: str = "",
   304	        tier: Tier = Tier.FRONTIER,
   305	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   306	        system_prompt: str = "",
   307	        workspace: Optional[Path] = None,   # default: per-task dir under ~/.metaharness/workspaces
   308	        binary: Optional[str] = None,       # override path (tests use a stub script)
   309	        extra_env: Optional[dict[str, str]] = None,
   310	        timeout_s: Optional[float] = None,  # None = task-type-aware default (issue #2)
   311	    ) -> None:
   312	        if cli not in CLI_ADAPTERS:
   313	            raise ValueError(f"unknown coding CLI '{cli}' (known: {sorted(CLI_ADAPTERS)})")
   314	        # model has two jobs kept strictly apart: `model` (display/matrix key,
   315	        # falls back to '<cli>-cli') vs `cli_model` (the explicit override the
   316	        # CLI receives; empty = the CLI's own configured default — a display
   317	        # placeholder must NEVER reach the command line)
   318	        super().__init__(worker_id=worker_id, tier=tier,
   319	                         model=model or f"{cli}-cli", keypair=keypair)
   320	        self.cli_model = model
   321	        self.cli = cli
   322	        self.adapter = CLI_ADAPTERS[cli]
   323	        self.system_prompt = system_prompt
   324	        self.workspace = Path(workspace) if workspace else None
   325	        self.binary = binary or self.adapter.binary
   326	        self.extra_env = extra_env or {}
   327	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s  # configured override; None = unset
   328	
   329	    def effective_timeout_s(self, task: Task) -> float:
   330	        """The timeout actually applied for one task: an explicit config
   331	        override wins flat across all task types; otherwise CODE_EDIT work
   332	        (a coding CLI implementing a plan) gets more room than a quick
   333	        one-shot text task (issue #2)."""
   334	        if self.timeout_s is not None:
   335	            return self.timeout_s
   336	        return self.BASE_TIMEOUT_S * TASK_TYPE_TIMEOUT_FACTOR.get(task.task_type, 1.0)
   337	
   338	    def _workspace_for(self, task: Task) -> Path:
   339	        explicit = (task.inputs or {}).get("_workspace")
   340	        ws = Path(explicit) if explicit else (
   341	            self.workspace or WORKSPACES_DIR / task.id
   342	        )
   343	        ws.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   344	        return ws
   345	
   346	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   347	        workspace = self._workspace_for(task)
   348	        prompt = _render_prompt(task)
   349	        argv, stdin_text = self.adapter.build(self, prompt, workspace)
   350	        # Carry the full outer-host chain into nested harnesses. This blocks
   351	        # direct recursion and cycles such as Codex -> Pi -> Codex before spawn.
   352	        env = {
   353	            **os.environ,
   354	            **self.extra_env,
   355	            **child_host_environment(self.cli),
   356	        }
   357	
   358	        try:
   359	            proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
   360	                *argv,
   361	                cwd=workspace,
   362	                env=env,
   363	                # Coding CLIs routinely spawn shells, tests, and helper agents.
   364	                # Give the attempt its own group so timeout/cancellation cannot
   365	                # leave descendants mutating the workspace after escalation.
   366	                start_new_session=True,
   367	                stdin=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE if stdin_text is not None else asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   368	                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   369	                stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   370	            )
   371	        except OSError as exc:
   372	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: cannot launch '{self.binary}': {exc}") from exc
   373	
   374	        eff = self.effective_timeout_s(task)
   375	        try:
   376	            stdout_b, stderr_b = await asyncio.wait_for(
   377	                proc.communicate(stdin_text.encode() if stdin_text is not None else None),
   378	                timeout=eff,
   379	            )
   380	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   381	            await self._terminate_process_group(proc)
   382	            # :g not :.0f — subsecond test timeouts (e.g. 0.5) must not render as "0s"
   383	            raise WorkerTimeout(f"{self.cli}: timed out after {eff:g}s", timeout_s=eff)
   384	        except asyncio.CancelledError:
   385	            await asyncio.shield(self._terminate_process_group(proc))
   386	            raise
   387	
   388	        stdout = stdout_b.decode(errors="replace")
   389	        stderr = stderr_b.decode(errors="replace")
   390	        if proc.returncode != 0:
   391	            detail = (stderr or stdout).strip()[-2000:]
   392	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: exit {proc.returncode}: {detail}")
   393	
   394	        text, cost = self.adapter.parse(stdout)
   395	        from metaharness.harness.local import parse_output
   396	        # F3 (panel 2026-07-09, GLM P2): coding CLIs (codex/opencode) report cost
   397	        # 0.0 and no token usage, so CodeProposer charged ~nothing for the most
   398	        # expensive calls in the harness. No adapter surfaces a token count today,
   399	        # so ESTIMATE from character length (~4 chars/token) — a rough but non-zero
   400	        # figure so budget accounting reflects that these calls are not free.
   401	        tokens_in = len(prompt) // 4
   402	        tokens_out = len(text) // 4
   403	        return WorkerResult(
   404	            task_id=task.id,
   405	            worker_id=self.worker_id,
   406	            tier=self.tier,
   407	            model=self.model,
   408	            output=parse_output(text, expect_json=bool(task.output_schema)),
   409	            raw_text=text,
   410	            tokens_in=tokens_in,
   411	            tokens_out=tokens_out,
   412	            cost_usd=cost,
   413	            workspace_root=str(workspace),
   414	        )
   415	
   416	    @staticmethod
   417	    async def _terminate_process_group(proc: asyncio.subprocess.Process) -> None:
   418	        """Terminate and reap an attempt's complete POSIX process group."""
   419	        if proc.returncode is not None:
   420	            await proc.wait()
   421	            return
   422	        pgid = CodingAgentWorker._process_group_id(proc)
   423	        tracked = CodingAgentWorker._linux_descendant_pids(proc.pid)
   424	        CodingAgentWorker._signal_process_tree(proc, signal.SIGTERM, pgid, tracked)
   425	        try:
   426	            await asyncio.wait_for(proc.wait(), timeout=0.5)
   427	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   428	            pass
   429	        await asyncio.sleep(0.05)
   430	        tracked.update(CodingAgentWorker._linux_descendant_pids(proc.pid))

     2	from __future__ import annotations
     3	
     4	from contextvars import ContextVar, Token
     5	from typing import Any, Callable, Optional
     6	
     7	RunEventSink = Callable[[str, dict[str, Any]], None]
     8	
     9	_sink: ContextVar[Optional[RunEventSink]] = ContextVar("run_event_sink", default=None)
    10	
    11	
    12	def bind_run_event_sink(sink: Optional[RunEventSink]) -> Token:
    13	    return _sink.set(sink)
    14	
    15	
    16	def reset_run_event_sink(token: Token) -> None:
    17	    _sink.reset(token)
    18	
    19	
    20	def emit_run_event(kind: str, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    21	    sink = _sink.get()
    22	    if sink is not None:
    23	        sink(kind, payload)
     1	"""The uniform Runner interface every worker harness sits behind.
     2	
     3	The orchestrator never talks to a model directly — it talks to a Runner: a Task
     4	goes in, a WorkerResult comes out. Real LLM-backed harnesses, scripted mocks, and
     5	enrichment wrappers all present this same face, so the router and orchestrator can
     6	compose them freely.
     7	
     8	`BaseRunner.run` owns the cross-cutting concerns (OTel span, timing, error
     9	capture, result signing); concrete runners implement `_execute` only.
    10	"""
    11	from __future__ import annotations
    12	
    13	import time
    14	from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
    15	from typing import Optional
    16	
    17	from metaharness.core.types import Task, Tier, WorkerResult
    18	from metaharness.identity.canonical import canonical_bytes
    19	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    20	from metaharness.identity.registry import WorkerRegistry
    21	from metaharness.observability.tracing import tracer
    22	
    23	
    24	class WorkerTimeout(RuntimeError):
    25	    """A worker's `_execute` ran out of its allotted wall-clock time. Carries
    26	    the timeout actually applied (post task-type scaling / config override,
    27	    issue #2) so callers can report it without re-deriving it."""
    28	
    29	    def __init__(self, msg: str, timeout_s: float) -> None:
    30	        super().__init__(msg)
    31	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s
    32	
    33	
    34	CURRENT_RESULT_SIGNATURE_VERSION = 2
    35	
    36	
    37	def result_signing_bytes(result: WorkerResult, *, version: Optional[int] = None) -> bytes:
    38	    """The exact bytes a worker signs to vouch for a result.
    39	
    40	    Version 1 is the historical payload and remains readable so old journals do
    41	    not become unverifiable. Version 2 additionally attests ``workspace_root``
    42	    and ``timed_out``: both now affect control flow (automatic test execution and
    43	    timeout classification), so treating them as mutable bookkeeping would let a
    44	    valid signature bless attacker-selected behavior.
    45	    """
    46	    version = result.signature_version if version is None else version
    47	    payload = {
    48	        "kind": "worker_result",
    49	        "task_id": result.task_id,
    50	        "worker_id": result.worker_id,
    51	        "model": result.model,
    52	        "output": result.output,
    53	        "raw_text": result.raw_text,
    54	        "error": result.error,
    55	    }
    56	    if version == 2:
    57	        payload.update({
    58	            "signature_version": 2,
    59	            "timed_out": result.timed_out,
    60	            "workspace_root": result.workspace_root,
    61	        })
    62	    elif version != 1:
    63	        raise ValueError(f"unsupported worker-result signature version {version}")
    64	    return canonical_bytes(payload)
    65	
    66	
    67	def sign_result(result: WorkerResult, keypair: KeyPair) -> WorkerResult:
    68	    """(Re)sign a result in place. Enrichment wrappers that legitimately rewrite
    69	    a worker's output inside the same harness boundary re-sign with the worker's
    70	    own key so the signature keeps matching what is actually returned."""
    71	    result.signature_version = CURRENT_RESULT_SIGNATURE_VERSION
    72	    result.signature_b64 = keypair.sign(result_signing_bytes(result))
    73	    return result
    74	
    75	
    76	def verify_result(result: WorkerResult, registry: WorkerRegistry) -> bool:
    77	    """True iff the result carries a signature that verifies under the key
    78	    registered for its worker_id."""
    79	    if not result.signature_b64:
    80	        return False
    81	    try:
    82	        payload = result_signing_bytes(result)
    83	    except ValueError:
    84	        return False
    85	    return registry.verify_message(result.worker_id, payload, result.signature_b64)
    86	
    87	
    88	class Runner(ABC):
    89	    """Anything that can execute a Task. Wrappers wrap Runners and are Runners."""
    90	
    91	    worker_id: str
    92	    tier: Tier
    93	    model: str
    94	
    95	    @abstractmethod
    96	    async def run(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult: ...
    97	
    98	
    99	class BaseRunner(Runner):
   100	    """Span + timing + signing wrapper around a concrete `_execute`."""
   101	
   102	    def __init__(
   103	        self,
   104	        worker_id: str,
   105	        tier: Tier,
   106	        model: str,
   107	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   108	    ) -> None:
   109	        self.worker_id = worker_id
   110	        self.tier = tier
   111	        self.model = model
   112	        self.keypair = keypair
   113	
   114	    async def run(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   115	        with tracer().start_as_current_span("worker.run") as span:
   116	            span.set_attribute("worker.id", self.worker_id)
   117	            span.set_attribute("worker.tier", self.tier.value)
   118	            span.set_attribute("worker.model", self.model)
   119	            span.set_attribute("task.id", task.id)
   120	            span.set_attribute("task.type", task.task_type.value)
   121	            started = time.monotonic()
   122	            try:
   123	                result = await self._execute(task)
   124	            except Exception as exc:  # a failed attempt is data, not a crash
   125	                result = WorkerResult(
   126	                    task_id=task.id,
   127	                    worker_id=self.worker_id,
   128	                    tier=self.tier,
   129	                    model=self.model,
   130	                    error=f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}",
   131	                    timed_out=isinstance(exc, WorkerTimeout),  # issue #2
   132	                )
   133	            result.latency_s = time.monotonic() - started
   134	            if self.keypair is not None:
   135	                sign_result(result, self.keypair)
   136	            span.set_attribute("worker.tokens_in", result.tokens_in)
   137	            span.set_attribute("worker.tokens_out", result.tokens_out)
   138	            span.set_attribute("worker.cost_usd", result.cost_usd)
   139	            if result.error:
   140	                span.set_attribute("worker.error", result.error)
   141	            return result
   142	
   143	    @abstractmethod
   144	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult: ...
     1	"""Shared domain types for the meta-harness.
     2	
     3	These are the vocabulary the whole system speaks: tasks flow in, get routed to a
     4	capability tier, executed by a worker harness, verified, and (on failure) reflected
     5	on. Everything is a plain pydantic model so it serializes cleanly into the journal,
     6	the provenance log, and the WebUI API.
     7	"""
     8	from __future__ import annotations
     9	
    10	import time
    11	import uuid
    12	from enum import Enum
    13	from typing import Any, Optional
    14	
    15	from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, model_validator
    16	
    17	
    18	def _new_id(prefix: str) -> str:
    19	    return f"{prefix}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
    20	
    21	
    22	def now() -> float:
    23	    return time.time()
    24	
    25	
    26	class Tier(str, Enum):
    27	    """Capability tiers. The router picks the cheapest tier likely to succeed and
    28	    escalates on a verifiable failure signal."""
    29	
    30	    SMALL = "small"    # haiku / 8B-class: narrow, verifiable, single-pass work
    31	    MID = "mid"        # sonnet-class: multi-step but bounded
    32	    FRONTIER = "frontier"  # opus/fable-class: long-horizon, ambiguous, novel
    33	
    34	
    35	class TaskType(str, Enum):
    36	    """Coarse task taxonomy. Drives the capability matrix and the enrichment stack.
    37	    A prescribed workflow tags each step with one of these."""
    38	
    39	    CLASSIFY = "classify"
    40	    EXTRACT = "extract"
    41	    SUMMARIZE = "summarize"
    42	    TRANSFORM = "transform"
    43	    ARITHMETIC = "arithmetic"      # always tool-offloaded to code
    44	    CODE_EDIT = "code_edit"
    45	    REASONING = "reasoning"
    46	    PLANNING = "planning"
    47	    GENERAL = "general"
    48	
    49	
    50	class Verdict(str, Enum):
    51	    PASS = "pass"
    52	    FAIL = "fail"
    53	    UNVERIFIED = "unverified"      # no scorer could produce ground truth
    54	
    55	
    56	class MASTMode(str, Enum):
    57	    """Failure vocabulary from the MAST taxonomy (Berkeley, 2025). Used to label
    58	    failures consistently so the learning loop can cluster before fixing."""
    59	
    60	    # system / specification design (~44% of MAS failures)
    61	    DISOBEY_TASK_SPEC = "disobey_task_spec"
    62	    DISOBEY_ROLE_SPEC = "disobey_role_spec"
    63	    STEP_REPETITION = "step_repetition"
    64	    LOSE_HISTORY = "lose_history"
    65	    UNAWARE_TERMINATION = "unaware_termination"
    66	    # inter-agent misalignment (~32%)
    67	    IGNORE_INPUT = "ignore_input"
    68	    WITHHELD_INFO = "withheld_info"
    69	    MISMATCHED_ASSUMPTION = "mismatched_assumption"
    70	    # task verification & termination
    71	    PREMATURE_TERMINATION = "premature_termination"
    72	    NO_VERIFICATION = "no_verification"
    73	    INCORRECT_VERIFICATION = "incorrect_verification"
    74	    # operational (harness-level)
    75	    TOOL_ERROR = "tool_error"
    76	    SCHEMA_INVALID = "schema_invalid"
    77	    BUDGET_EXCEEDED = "budget_exceeded"
    78	    TIMEOUT = "timeout"          # issue #2: distinct from generic TOOL_ERROR
    79	    UNKNOWN = "unknown"
    80	
    81	
    82	class Task(BaseModel):
    83	    """A unit of work handed to a worker harness."""
    84	
    85	    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: _new_id("task"))
    86	    task_type: TaskType = TaskType.GENERAL
    87	    # explicit delegation contract (Anthropic multi-agent lesson): objective,
    88	    # output format, and boundaries are load-bearing, not decoration.
    89	    objective: str = ""
    90	    inputs: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    91	    output_schema: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None
    92	    boundaries: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    93	    # a checkable success signal, if one exists. Interpreted by the verifier.
    94	    success_check: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None
    95	    tier_hint: Optional[Tier] = None
    96	    # Human-friendly assignment constraints. ``worker_id`` is a hard pin;
    97	    # role/capabilities are requirements that any selected worker must satisfy.
    98	    role: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, exclude_if=lambda value: value is None)
    99	    required_capabilities: list[str] = Field(
   100	        default_factory=list, exclude_if=lambda value: not value
   101	    )
   102	    worker_id: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, exclude_if=lambda value: value is None)
   103	    max_attempts: int = 3
   104	    # tool names this task may call (small per-step subset, never the catalog)
   105	    tools: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
   106	    # Ask the orchestrator to attach a harness-owned, sandboxed test receipt.
   107	    # This never grants the worker a command-execution tool.
   108	    requires_execution_evidence: bool = False
   109	
   110	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   111	    def _assignment_is_unambiguous(self) -> "Task":
   112	        self.role = (self.role.strip() or None) if self.role else None
   113	        self.worker_id = (self.worker_id.strip() or None) if self.worker_id else None
   114	        self.required_capabilities = list(dict.fromkeys(
   115	            value.strip() for value in self.required_capabilities if value.strip()
   116	        ))
   117	        if self.worker_id and self.tier_hint is not None:
   118	            raise ValueError("worker_id and tier_hint cannot be combined")
   119	        return self
   120	
   121	
   122	class WorkerResult(BaseModel):
   123	    """What a worker harness returns for one attempt."""
   124	
   125	    task_id: str
   126	    worker_id: str
   127	    tier: Tier
   128	    model: str
   129	    output: Any = None
   130	    raw_text: str = ""
   131	    tool_calls: list[dict[str, Any]] = Field(default_factory=list)
   132	    tokens_in: int = 0
   133	    tokens_out: int = 0
   134	    cost_usd: float = 0.0
   135	    latency_s: float = 0.0
   136	    error: Optional[str] = None
   137	    # Legacy v1 signatures covered only the worker's textual result. New v2
   138	    # signatures also attest the execution-relevant metadata below. Keeping an
   139	    # explicit version lets old journal signatures remain verifiable without
   140	    # allowing their unsigned workspace_root to select code for execution.
   141	    signature_version: int = 1
   142	    # Derived metadata (issue #2): set by BaseRunner.run when `error` came from
   143	    # a WorkerTimeout. It is covered by v2 signatures.
   144	    timed_out: bool = False
   145	    # the directory this worker's file side-effects land in (builtin tool jail
   146	    # root or coding-CLI cwd), recorded by the runner that KNOWS it — evidence
   147	    # collection and run packaging must never infer this from cwd or guess
   148	    workspace_root: str = ""
   149	    # detached signature over `result_signing_bytes(...)`, made with the worker's
   150	    # registered key, so the orchestrator can confirm who produced this result.
   151	    signature_b64: Optional[str] = None
   152	
   153	
   154	class VerificationResult(BaseModel):
   155	    verdict: Verdict
   156	    score: float = 0.0            # 0..1
   157	    detail: str = ""
   158	    failure_mode: Optional[MASTMode] = None
   159	    scorer: str = ""             # which scorer produced this (execution/schema/judge)
   160	    latency_s: float = 0.0        # verifier wall time; execution checks charge this to Budget
   161	
   162	
   163	class Attempt(BaseModel):
   164	    """One pass through execute+verify. A task may take several before it passes
   165	    or exhausts its budget."""
   166	
   167	    n: int
   168	    result: WorkerResult
   169	    verification: VerificationResult
   170	    reflection: Optional[str] = None   # written only after a failed attempt
   171	
   172	
   173	class TaskOutcome(BaseModel):
   174	    """The full record for a task: every attempt and the final disposition."""
   175	
   176	    task: Task
   177	    attempts: list[Attempt] = Field(default_factory=list)
   178	    final_verdict: Verdict = Verdict.UNVERIFIED
   179	    final_output: Any = None
   180	    total_cost_usd: float = 0.0
   181	    escalations: int = 0
   182	    started_at: float = Field(default_factory=now)
   183	    ended_at: Optional[float] = None

     1	"""TaskExecutor: the execute→verify→reflect→escalate loop for one task.
     2	
     3	This is the heart of the meta-harness. One call runs a task to completion:
     4	
     5	    route (cheapest capable) → run → confirm authenticity → verify →
     6	    on FAIL: reflect, retry timeout once in-tier, otherwise escalate → record everything
     7	
     8	Every attempt updates the capability matrix (verified outcomes only), charges
     9	the budget, and is journaled into the provenance chain under the orchestrator's
    10	own key. Guardrails from core.budget stop runaway loops: hard budget ceilings,
    11	plateau detection across attempts, and step-repetition dedup.
    12	"""
    13	from __future__ import annotations
    14	
    15	import asyncio
    16	import time
    17	from typing import Any, Awaitable, Callable, Optional

    48	# a reflector turns a failed attempt into advice for the next one
    49	Reflector = Callable[[Task, Attempt], Optional[str]]
    50	# a judge grades an UNVERIFIED output against its contract (rubric-judge slot
    51	# of the verifier hierarchy); async because it calls a worker
    52	Judge = Callable[..., "object"]
    53	ExecutionVerifier = Callable[
    54	    [Task, WorkerResult], Awaitable[Optional[VerificationResult]]
    55	]
    56	WorkspaceVerifier = Callable[[str], Awaitable[Optional[VerificationResult]]]
    57	TaskEventSink = Callable[[str, dict[str, Any]], None]

    60	class TaskExecutor:
    61	    def __init__(
    62	        self,
    63	        router: Router,
    64	        registry: Optional[WorkerRegistry] = None,
    65	        provenance: Optional[ProvenanceLog] = None,
    66	        orchestrator_keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,

    70	        observer: Optional[Callable[[TaskOutcome], None]] = None,
    71	        judge: Optional[Judge] = None,
    72	        execution_verifier: Optional[ExecutionVerifier] = verify_code_edit_execution,
    73	        workspace_root: str = "",
    74	        workspace_verifier: Optional[WorkspaceVerifier] = run_workspace_execution,
    75	    ) -> None:
    76	        self.router = router
    77	        self.registry = registry
    78	        self.provenance = provenance
    79	        self.orchestrator_keypair = orchestrator_keypair
    80	        self.budget = budget
    81	        self.reflector = reflector
    82	        self.playbook_hints = playbook_hints
    83	        self.observer = observer
    84	        self.judge = judge
    85	        self.execution_verifier = execution_verifier
    86	        self.workspace_root = workspace_root
    87	        self.workspace_verifier = workspace_verifier
    88	        if provenance is not None and orchestrator_keypair is None:
    89	            raise ValueError("provenance logging needs the orchestrator keypair")
    90	
    91	    def _record(self, action: str, detail: dict) -> None:
    92	        if self.provenance is not None:
    93	            self.provenance.append(
    94	                "orchestrator", action, detail, keypair=self.orchestrator_keypair
    95	            )
    96	
    97	    def _attempt_task(self, task: Task, advice: list[str]) -> Task:
    98	        """The task as sent for this attempt — original contract plus accumulated
    99	        reflections/playbook hints in the boundaries."""
   100	        if not advice:
   101	            return task
   102	        variant = task.model_copy(deep=True)
   103	        variant.boundaries = list(task.boundaries) + advice
   104	        return variant
   105	
   106	    async def execute(
   107	        self, task: Task, *, event_sink: Optional[TaskEventSink] = None
   108	    ) -> TaskOutcome:
   109	        """Execute one task, optionally emitting live attempt/verification events.
   110	
   111	        The callback is synchronous by design: the workflow journal fsyncs each
   112	        event before execution moves past the corresponding transition.
   113	        """
   114	        def emit(kind: str, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
   115	            if event_sink is not None:
   116	                event_sink(kind, payload)
   117

   119	        plateau = PlateauDetector()
   120	        seen_signatures: set[str] = set()
   121	        excluded_tiers: set[Tier] = set()
   122	        # A timeout is an operational signal, not evidence that the tier lacks
   123	        # capability. Give each routed tier one retry before excluding it; the
   124	        # set keeps repeated timeouts from turning max_attempts into an
   125	        # unbounded same-tier loop (issue #11).
