     1	"""Durable, append-only workflow run events.
     2	
     3	New runs write one versioned canonical stream.  ``entries()`` is an explicit
     4	projection onto the historical ``JournalEntry`` vocabulary so existing package,
     5	harvest, and web readers remain compatible without duplicate on-disk records.
     6	"""
     7	from __future__ import annotations
     8	
     9	import contextlib
    10	import json
    11	import math
    12	import os
    13	import stat
    14	import time
    15	from pathlib import Path
    16	from typing import Any, Iterator, Literal, Optional
    17	
    18	import fcntl
    19	from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator, model_validator
    20	
    21	
    22	CANONICAL_KINDS = frozenset({
    23	    "run.started", "step.ready", "step.started",
    24	    "attempt.assigned", "attempt.started",
    25	    "tool.requested", "tool.completed",
    26	    "verification.started", "verification.completed",
    27	    "approval.required", "approval.resolved",
    28	    "step.completed", "step.failed", "step.skipped",
    29	    "run.completed", "run.failed",
    30	})
    31	
    32	
    33	class RunEvent(BaseModel):
    34	    """One event in the canonical v1 run stream."""
    35	
    36	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
    37	    seq: int = Field(ge=0)
    38	    at: float
    39	    kind: str
    40	    run_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
    41	    snapshot_digest: str = Field(pattern=r"^[0-9a-f]{64}$")
    42	    step_id: Optional[str] = None
    43	    attempt_id: Optional[str] = None
    44	    payload: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    45	
    46	    model_config = {"extra": "forbid"}
    47	
    48	    @field_validator("at")
    49	    @classmethod
    50	    def _finite_timestamp(cls, value: float) -> float:
    51	        if not math.isfinite(value):
    52	            raise ValueError("event timestamp must be finite")
    53	        return value
    54	
    55	    @field_validator("kind")
    56	    @classmethod
    57	    def _known_kind(cls, value: str) -> str:
    58	        if value not in CANONICAL_KINDS:
    59	            raise ValueError(f"unknown canonical event kind {value!r}")
    60	        return value
    61	
    62	    @model_validator(mode="after")
    63	    def _required_identity_fields(self) -> "RunEvent":
    64	        if self.kind.startswith("run."):
    65	            if self.step_id is not None or self.attempt_id is not None:
    66	                raise ValueError("run events cannot carry step/attempt IDs")
    67	        elif not self.step_id:
    68	            raise ValueError(f"{self.kind} requires a step ID")
    69	        if self.kind.startswith(("attempt.", "tool.", "verification.")):
    70	            if not self.attempt_id:
    71	                raise ValueError(f"{self.kind} requires an attempt ID")
    72	        return self
    73	
    74	
    75	class JournalEntry(BaseModel):
    76	    """Historical event shape returned by :meth:`Journal.entries`.
    77	
    78	    It intentionally keeps the old permissive defaults because archived
    79	    journals with omitted ``step_id``/``payload`` remain valid inputs.
    80	    """
    81	
    82	    seq: int
    83	    at: float
    84	    kind: str
    85	    run_id: str
    86	    step_id: Optional[str] = None
    87	    payload: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    88	
    89	
    90	def _reject_duplicate_keys(pairs: list[tuple[str, Any]]) -> dict[str, Any]:
    91	    result: dict[str, Any] = {}
    92	    for key, value in pairs:
    93	        if key in result:
    94	            raise ValueError(f"duplicate JSON key {key!r}")
    95	        result[key] = value
    96	    return result
    97	
    98	
    99	def _reject_constant(value: str) -> None:
   100	    raise ValueError(f"non-finite JSON number {value}")
   101	
   102	
   103	def _parse_line(line: str, *, line_no: int) -> dict[str, Any]:
   104	    try:
   105	        value = json.loads(
   106	            line,
   107	            object_pairs_hook=_reject_duplicate_keys,
   108	            parse_constant=_reject_constant,
   109	        )
   110	    except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as exc:
   111	        raise ValueError(f"invalid journal JSON at line {line_no}: {exc}") from exc
   112	    if not isinstance(value, dict):
   113	        raise ValueError(f"journal line {line_no} must be a JSON object")
   114	    return value
   115	
   116	
   117	def _legacy_projection(event: RunEvent) -> Optional[JournalEntry]:
   118	    kind = event.kind
   119	    payload = dict(event.payload)
   120	    projected: Optional[str]
   121	    if kind in {"run.started", "step.started"}:
   122	        projected = kind
   123	    elif kind == "verification.completed":
   124	        projected = "step.attempt"
   125	    elif kind == "approval.required":
   126	        projected = "hitl.requested"
   127	    elif kind == "approval.resolved":
   128	        projected = "hitl.resolved"
   129	    elif kind in {"step.completed", "step.failed", "step.skipped"}:
   130	        projected = kind
   131	    elif kind in {"run.completed", "run.failed"}:
   132	        projected = "run.finished"
   133	        payload.setdefault("status", "completed" if kind == "run.completed" else "failed")
   134	    else:
   135	        projected = None
   136	    if projected is None:
   137	        return None
   138	    return JournalEntry(
   139	        seq=event.seq,
   140	        at=event.at,
   420	                    )
   421	                except ValueError as exc:
   422	                    # a bad input reference must FAIL the run visibly — a stuck
   423	                    # "running" state with no journal trail is the worst outcome
   424	                    state.status = RunStatus.FAILED
   425	                    state.failed_step = step.id
   426	                    journal.append_event("step.failed", run_id, step_id=step.id,
   427	                                         payload={"reason": str(exc)})
   428	                    journal.append_event(
   429	                        "run.failed", run_id,
   430	                        payload={"status": "failed", "failed_step": step.id,
   431	                                 "reason": f"step {step.id}: {exc}"},
   432	                    )
   433	                    return state
   434	                journal.append_event(
   435	                    "step.started", run_id, step_id=step.id,
   436	                    payload={"task_id": task.id},
   437	                )
   438	
   439	                try:
   440	                    prior_attempts = sum(
   441	                        event.kind == "attempt.assigned" and event.step_id == step.id
   442	                        for event in journal.events()
   443	                    )
   444	                    def event_sink(kind: str, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
   445	                        attempt = payload.get("n")
   446	                        journal.append_event(
   447	                            kind, run_id, step_id=step.id, payload=payload,
   448	                            attempt_id=(
   449	                                f"{step.id}-attempt-{prior_attempts + int(attempt)}"
   450	                                if attempt is not None else None
   451	                            ),
   452	                        )
   453	
   454	                    params = inspect.signature(self.executor.execute).parameters
   455	                    if "event_sink" in params:
   456	                        outcome = await self.executor.execute(task, event_sink=event_sink)
   457	                    else:  # compatibility with small test/custom executors
   458	                        outcome = await self.executor.execute(task)
   459	                except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — same visibility rule
   460	                    state.status = RunStatus.FAILED
   461	                    state.failed_step = step.id
   462	                    journal.append_event(
   463	                        "step.failed", run_id, step_id=step.id,
   464	                        payload={"reason": f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"},
   465	                    )
   466	                    journal.append_event(
   467	                        "run.failed", run_id,
   468	                        payload={"status": "failed", "failed_step": step.id,
   469	                                 "reason": f"step {step.id} crashed: {exc}"},
   470	                    )
   471	                    return state
   472	                record = StepRecord(
   473	                    step_id=step.id,
   474	                    verdict=outcome.final_verdict,
   475	                    output=outcome.final_output,
   140	        journal = Journal(path=journal_path, canonical=True)
   141	        digest = _snapshot_digest(spec, blueprint_snapshot)
   142	        state = RunState(
   143	            run_id=run_id,
   144	            workflow=spec.name,
   145	            context=context or {},
   146	            blueprint_ref=blueprint_ref,
   147	            blueprint_snapshot=blueprint_snapshot,
   148	            snapshot_digest=digest,
   149	        )
   150	        payload: dict[str, Any] = {
   151	            "workflow": spec.model_dump(mode="json"),
   152	            "context": state.context,
   153	            "snapshot_digest": digest,
   154	        }
   155	        if state.blueprint_ref is not None:
   156	            payload["blueprint_ref"] = state.blueprint_ref
   157	        if state.blueprint_snapshot is not None:
   158	            payload["blueprint_snapshot"] = state.blueprint_snapshot
   159	        journal.initialize(run_id, payload, snapshot_digest=digest)
   160	        self._runs[run_id] = (spec, state, journal)
   161	        return state
   162	
   163	    def state(self, run_id: str) -> RunState:
   164	        return self._runs[run_id][1]
   165	
   166	    def journal(self, run_id: str) -> Journal:
   167	        return self._runs[run_id][2]
   168	
   169	    def runs(self) -> list[RunState]:
   170	        return [state for _, state, _ in self._runs.values()]
   171	
   172	    @staticmethod
   173	    def _archive_path(journal: Journal) -> Optional[Path]:
   174	        return (
   175	            journal._path.with_name(journal._path.stem + ".archive.json")
   176	            if journal._path is not None
   177	            else None
   178	        )
   179	
   180	    @classmethod
   181	    def _read_archive_metadata(cls, journal: Journal) -> Optional[float]:
   182	        path = cls._archive_path(journal)
   183	        if path is None or not path.exists():
   184	            return None
   185	        value = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   186	        archived_at = value.get("archived_at") if isinstance(value, dict) else None
   187	        if not isinstance(archived_at, (int, float)) or isinstance(archived_at, bool):
   188	            raise ValueError("invalid run archive metadata")
   189	        return float(archived_at)
   190	
   191	    @classmethod
   192	    def _write_archive_metadata(
   193	        cls, journal: Journal, archived_at: Optional[float]
   194	    ) -> None:
   195	        path = cls._archive_path(journal)
   196	        if path is None:
   197	            return
   198	        if archived_at is None:
   199	            path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
   200	            dir_fd = os.open(path.parent, os.O_RDONLY)
   201	            try:
   202	                os.fsync(dir_fd)
   203	            finally:
   204	                os.close(dir_fd)
   205	            return
   206	        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   207	        fd, tmp_name = tempfile.mkstemp(
   208	            dir=path.parent, prefix=f".{path.name}.", suffix=".tmp"
   209	        )
   210	        tmp_path = Path(tmp_name)
   211	        try:
   212	            with os.fdopen(fd, "w", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
   213	                json.dump({"archived_at": archived_at}, handle)
   214	                handle.flush()
   215	                os.fsync(handle.fileno())
   216	            os.chmod(tmp_path, 0o600)
   217	            os.replace(tmp_path, path)
   218	            dir_fd = os.open(path.parent, os.O_RDONLY)
   219	            try:
   220	                os.fsync(dir_fd)

    31	def _source(**changes):
    32	    values = {
    33	        "source_id": "repo-instructions",
    34	        "kind": ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
    35	        "scope": ContextScope(project_id="meta-harness"),
    36	        "trust": ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
    37	        "content_hash": "sha256:" + "1" * 64,
    38	        "selection_reason": "required repository contract",
    39	        "sensitivity": Sensitivity.PUBLIC,
    40	        "fetchable": False,
    41	    }
    42	    values.update(changes)
    43	    return ContextSourceRef(**values)
    44	
    45	
    46	def _section(**changes):
    47	    source = changes.pop("source", _source())
    48	    values = {
    49	        "section_type": ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
    50	        "stable_id": "system-contract",
    51	        "source": source,
    52	        "source_hash": source.content_hash,
    53	        "trust": source.trust,
    54	        "content": "You are a bounded worker.",
    55	        "original_tokens": 7,
    56	        "selected_tokens": 7,
    57	        "compressed_tokens": 7,
    58	        "budget_tokens": 100,
    59	        "ordering_priority": 0,
    60	        "sensitivity": source.sensitivity,
    61	        "compression_action": CompressionAction.NONE,
    62	    }
    63	    values.update(changes)
    64	    return ContextSection(**values)

    67	@pytest.mark.parametrize(
    68	    "changes",
    69	    [
    70	        {"unknown": "field"},
    71	        {"content_hash": None, "high_water_mark": None},
    72	        {"content_hash": "sha256:" + "1" * 64, "high_water_mark": "event:9"},
    73	        {"fetchable": True, "artifact_ref": None},
    74	        {"fetchable": False, "artifact_ref": "artifact:secret"},
    75	    ],
    76	)
    77	def test_source_contract_fails_closed_on_unknown_or_ambiguous_inputs(changes):
    78	    with pytest.raises(ValidationError):
    79	        _source(**changes)

    90	    with pytest.raises(ValidationError):
    91	        _section(source_hash="sha256:" + "2" * 64)
    92	    with pytest.raises(ValidationError):

    96	            content="",
    97	            selected_tokens=0,

   100	            omission_reason="budget",

   104	def test_version_bindings_reject_self_parent_lineage_and_unknown_axes():
   105	    values = {
   106	        "model_portfolio_version": "portfolio:1",
   107	        "harness_version": "h:1",
   108	        "evaluator_version": "e:1",
   109	        "weight_snapshot_version": None,
   110	        "memory_snapshot_version": "memory:4",
   111	        "evidence_snapshot_version": "evidence:9",
   112	        "candidate_version": "candidate:2",
   113	        "parent_candidate_version": "candidate:1",
   114	    }
   115	    assert ContextVersionBindings(**values).weight_snapshot_version is None
   116	    with pytest.raises(ValidationError):
   117	        ContextVersionBindings(**{**values, "parent_candidate_version": "candidate:2"})
   118	    with pytest.raises(ValidationError):
   119	        ContextVersionBindings(**{**values, "deployment_version": "prod"})

   122	def test_tier_section_budgets_are_deterministic_complete_and_tier_specific():
   123	    sections = [
   124	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   125	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   126	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY,
   127	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   128	    ]
   129	    small = allocate_section_budgets(sections, 1001, tier="small")
   130	    frontier = allocate_section_budgets(sections, 1001, tier="frontier")
   131	    assert small == allocate_section_budgets(sections, 1001, tier="small")
   132	    assert sum(small) == sum(frontier) == 1001
   133	    assert small != frontier
   134	    assert small[0] > frontier[0]
   135	    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
   136	        allocate_section_budgets(sections, -1, tier="small")

   139	def test_fit_receipt_is_deterministic_reconstructable_and_compatible():
   140	    messages = [
   141	        {"role": "system", "content": "contract " * 40},
   142	        {"role": "user", "content": "head-marker " + "middle " * 4000 + " tail-marker"},
   143	        {"role": "tool", "content": "tool-head " + "observation " * 4000 + " tool-tail"},
   144	        {"role": "user", "content": "final response contract"},
   145	    ]
   146	    original = copy.deepcopy(messages)
   147	
   148	    first = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   149	        messages,
   150	        budget_tokens=2600,
   151	        model_id="local-model",
   152	        harness_version="git:abc123",
   153	        policy_version="context-v1",
   154	    )
   155	    second = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   156	        copy.deepcopy(messages),
   157	        budget_tokens=2600,
   158	        model_id="local-model",
   159	        harness_version="git:abc123",
   160	        policy_version="context-v1",
   161	    )
   162	
   163	    assert messages == original
   164	    assert first.messages == fit_messages(messages, 2600)
   165	    assert first.model_dump_json() == second.model_dump_json()
   166	    assert first.manifest.reconstruct_messages() == first.redacted_messages
   167	    assert (
   168	        first.manifest.reconstruct_redacted_envelope().content_hash
   169	        == json.loads(first.manifest.redacted_envelope_json)["content_hash"]
   170	    )
   171	    assert first.envelope.content_hash == second.envelope.content_hash
   172	    assert first.manifest.manifest_hash == second.manifest.manifest_hash
   173	    assert first.messages[0] == messages[0]
   174	    assert first.messages[-1] == messages[-1]
   175	    compressed = [r for r in first.manifest.compression_receipts if r.action != "none"]
   176	    assert compressed
   177	    assert all(r.before_hash != r.after_hash for r in compressed)
   178	    assert "tool-head" in first.messages[2]["content"]
   179	    assert "tool-tail" in first.messages[2]["content"]
   180

   182	def test_receipt_honestly_records_legacy_head_tail_growth_near_floor():
   183	    receipt = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   184	        [
   185	            {"role": "system", "content": "system"},
   186	            {"role": "user", "content": "x" * 410},
   187	            {"role": "user", "content": "final"},
   188	        ],
   189	        budget_tokens=100,
   190	        model_id="m",
   191	        harness_version="h",
   192	    )
   193	    transformations = [
   194	        item for item in receipt.manifest.compression_receipts
   195	        if item.action == CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL
   196	    ]
   197	    assert transformations
   198	    assert any(item.final_tokens > item.original_tokens for item in transformations)

   201	def test_manifest_redacts_sensitive_values_without_changing_live_messages():
   202	    secret = "sk-live-super-secret"
   203	    messages = [
   204	        {"role": "system", "content": "system contract"},
   205	        {"role": "user", "content": f"token={secret}"},
   206	    ]
   207	    receipt = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   208	        messages,
   209	        budget_tokens=10_000,
   210	        model_id="m",
   211	        harness_version="h",
   212	        redaction_values=[secret],
   213	    )
   214	
   215	    assert receipt.messages == messages
   216	    assert secret in receipt.messages[1]["content"]
   217	    assert secret not in receipt.manifest.model_dump_json()
   218	    assert secret not in receipt.manifest.reconstruct_redacted_envelope().model_dump_json()
   219	    assert receipt.manifest.reconstruct_messages()[1]["content"] == "token=[REDACTED]"
   220	    assert receipt.manifest.redaction_count == 1
   221

   223	def test_redaction_prefers_longest_secret_and_redacts_secret_keys():
   224	    short = "credential-short"
   225	    long = "credential-short-production-999"
   226	    receipt = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   227	        [
   228	            {"role": "system", "content": "system"},
   229	            {"role": "user", "content": f"value={long}"},
   230	        ],
   231	        budget_tokens=10_000,
   232	        model_id="m",
   233	        harness_version="h",
   234	        redaction_values=[short, long],
   235	        tool_schemas=[{"type": "function", "function": {long: "must not persist"}}],
   236	    )
   237	    persisted = receipt.manifest.model_dump_json()
   238	    assert short not in persisted
   239	    assert long not in persisted
   240	    assert "production-999" not in persisted
   241	    assert "[REDACTED_KEY_" in persisted

   262	async def test_local_worker_emits_shadow_manifest_and_preserves_request_bytes():
   263	    seen = {}
   264	
   265	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   266	        seen["body"] = json.loads(request.content)
   267	        return httpx.Response(
   268	            200,
   269	            json={
   270	                "choices": [{"message": {"content": "done"}}],
   271	                "usage": {"prompt_tokens": 3, "completion_tokens": 1},
   272	            },
   273	        )
   274	
   275	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
   276	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker(

   374	            return "untrusted tool observation"

   396	            )

codex
A blocking integration issue has surfaced: the worker-side event hook is attempt-scoped, but the durable workflow journal rejects `context.manifest` as an unknown event kind. Because the spec also preserves telemetry-sink exception swallowing and forbids changes outside owned paths, the proposed “journal” would silently disappear in real workflow execution. I’m continuing through caller/test couplings and the assembler’s structural contracts before assigning the final severity.

     1	"""OpenAI-compatible local worker tests.
     2	
     3	Unit tests run against an httpx MockTransport that speaks the real chat-completions

    20	def completion_response(content: str, prompt_tokens: int = 30, completion_tokens: int = 12):
    21	    return {
    22	        "id": "chatcmpl-1",
    23	        "object": "chat.completion",
    24	        "choices": [{"index": 0, "message": {"role": "assistant", "content": content}}],
    25	        "usage": {
    26	            "prompt_tokens": prompt_tokens,
    27	            "completion_tokens": completion_tokens,
    28	            "total_tokens": prompt_tokens + completion_tokens,
    29	        },
    30	    }
    31	
    32	
    33	def make_worker(handler, **kw) -> OpenAICompatWorker:
    34	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
    35	    return OpenAICompatWorker(
    36	        "local-1", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="minicpm5-1b", client=client, **kw
    37	    )
    38

    40	async def test_request_shape_and_text_output():
    41	    seen = {}
    42	
    43	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
    44	        seen["url"] = str(request.url)
    45	        seen["body"] = json.loads(request.content)
    46	        return httpx.Response(200, json=completion_response("The answer is yes."))
    47	
    48	    worker = make_worker(handler, thinking=False)
    49	    task = Task(
    50	        task_type=TaskType.CLASSIFY,
    51	        objective="Is this review positive?",
    52	        inputs={"text": "loved it", "_hidden": "not sent"},
    53	        boundaries=["answer only from the given text"],
    54	    )
    55	    result = await worker.run(task)
    56	
    57	    assert seen["url"] == "http://fake/v1/chat/completions"
    58	    body = seen["body"]
    59	    assert body["model"] == "minicpm5-1b"
    60	    assert body["chat_template_kwargs"] == {"enable_thinking": False}
    61	    assert body["messages"][0]["role"] == "system"
    62	    assert "answer only from the given text" in body["messages"][0]["content"]
    63	    assert "loved it" in body["messages"][1]["content"]
    64	    assert "_hidden" not in body["messages"][1]["content"]
    65	    assert result.output == "The answer is yes."
    66	    assert result.tokens_in == 30 and result.tokens_out == 12
    67	    assert result.error is None
    68

    70	async def test_json_schema_output_parsed():
    71	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
    72	        body = json.loads(request.content)
    73	        assert body["response_format"] == {"type": "json_object"}
    74	        return httpx.Response(
    75	            200, json=completion_response('```json\n{"label": "positive", "confidence": 0.93}\n```')
    76	        )
    77	
    78	    worker = make_worker(handler)
    79	    task = Task(
    80	        objective="classify",
    81	        output_schema={"type": "object", "required": ["label"], "properties": {"label": {"type": "string"}}},
    82	    )
    83	    result = await worker.run(task)
    84	    assert result.output == {"label": "positive", "confidence": 0.93}

    96	async def test_http_timeout_becomes_structured_worker_timeout():
    97	    """issue #2 parity: an OpenAICompatWorker timeout must journal as
    98	    timed_out=True, same as CodingAgentWorker — without this it silently
    99	    looked like a generic tool_error."""
   100	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   101	        raise httpx.ConnectTimeout("timed out", request=request)

   104	    result = await worker.run(Task(objective="x"))

   119	async def test_tool_httpx_timeout_is_not_a_model_timeout():
   120	    """issue #2 panel (Claude+codex P2): the WorkerTimeout catch wraps ONLY the
   121	    model call — an httpx timeout escaping a TOOL handler must surface as a
   122	    tool error, never as 'the model timed out after Ns' with the wrong
   123	    duration."""
   124	
   125	    class TimeoutToolRegistry:
   126	        workspace_root = ""
   127	
   128	        def openai_schemas(self, names):
   129	            return [{"type": "function",
   130	                     "function": {"name": "probe", "parameters": {}}}]
   131	
   132	        async def call(self, name, arguments, focus=""):
   133	            raise httpx.ReadTimeout("tool transport stalled")
   134	
   135	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   136	        return httpx.Response(200, json={
   137	            "choices": [{"index": 0, "message": {
   138	                "role": "assistant", "content": None,
   139	                "tool_calls": [{"id": "c1", "function":
   140	                                {"name": "probe", "arguments": "{}"}}]}}],
   141	            "usage": {"prompt_tokens": 1, "completion_tokens": 1},
   142	        })
   143	
   144	    worker = make_worker(handler, tool_registry=TimeoutToolRegistry())
   145	    result = await worker.run(Task(objective="x", tools=["probe"]))
   146	    assert result.timed_out is False
   147	    assert result.error is not None and "ReadTimeout" in result.error
   148	    assert "timed out after" not in result.error  # never claims a model timeout

   151	def test_parse_output_variants():
   152	    assert parse_output("plain text", expect_json=False) == "plain text"
   153	    assert parse_output('{"a": 1}', expect_json=True) == {"a": 1}
   154	    assert parse_output('```json\n{"a": 1}\n```', expect_json=True) == {"a": 1}
   155	    assert parse_output('Sure! Here it is: {"a": 1} hope that helps', expect_json=True) == {"a": 1}
   156	    assert parse_output("not json at all", expect_json=True) == "not json at all"

    17	def _stub(tmp_path: Path, name: str, script: str) -> str:
    18	    path = tmp_path / name
    19	    path.write_text(f"#!/bin/sh\n{script}\n")
    20	    path.chmod(path.stat().st_mode | stat.S_IXUSR)
    21	    return str(path)

    26	    defaults.update(kw)

   184	    from metaharness.tools import default_registry
   185	    from metaharness.web import HarnessState
   186	    from metaharness.workflows import RunStatus, get_template
   187	    from metaharness.workflows.package import build_package_bytes
   188	
   189	    workspace = tmp_path / "workspace"
   190	    workspace.mkdir()
   191	    artifact = workspace / "artifact.txt"
   192	    artifact.write_text("seed\n")
   193	
   194	    subscription_binary = _stub(tmp_path, "subscription-claude", r'''
   195	prompt=$(cat)
   196	content=$(tr '\n' ' ' < artifact.txt)
   197	case "$prompt" in
   198	  *recommendation*checks*findings*) printf '{"result":"{\\"recommendation\\":\\"ship\\",\\"checks\\":[{\\"area\\":\\"spec\\",\\"result\\":\\"pass\\",\\"evidence\\":\\"implemented artifact.txt\\"},{\\"area\\":\\"tests\\",\\"result\\":\\"pass\\",\\"evidence\\":\\"verification passed\\"},{\\"area\\":\\"edge cases\\",\\"result\\":\\"pass\\",\\"evidence\\":\\"no uncovered requirement\\"},{\\"area\\":\\"plan\\",\\"result\\":\\"pass\\",\\"evidence\\":\\"no deviation\\"}],\\"findings\\":[]}"}\n' ;;
   199	  *all_met*) printf '{"result":"{\\"all_met\\":true,\\"criteria\\":[{\\"criterion\\":\\"artifact\\",\\"met\\":true,\\"evidence\\":\\"%s\\"}]}"}\n' "$content" ;;
   200	  *) printf '{"result":"saw artifact.txt: %s"}\n' "$content" ;;
   201	esac
   202	''')
   203	    coding_binary = _stub(tmp_path, "coding-claude", r'''
   204	prompt=$(cat)
   205	case "$prompt" in
   206	  *"Implement the approved plan"*)
   207	    printf 'implemented\n' >> artifact.txt
   208	    result='implemented artifact.txt' ;;
   209	  *) result='technical plan for artifact.txt' ;;
   210	esac
   211	printf '{"result":"%s"}\n' "$result"
   212	''')
   213	
   214	    sub_key = KeyPair.generate()
   215	    code_key = KeyPair.generate()
   216	    subscription = SubscriptionWorker(
   217	        "subscription", cli="claude", tier=Tier.MID,
   218	        keypair=sub_key, binary=subscription_binary,
   219	    )
   220	    coding = CodingAgentWorker(
   221	        "coding", cli="claude", tier=Tier.FRONTIER,
   222	        keypair=code_key, workspace=workspace, binary=coding_binary,
   223	    )
   224	    state = HarnessState()
   225	    state.tools = default_registry(workspace)
   226	    state.register_worker(subscription, sub_key, tiers=["mid"])
   227	    state.register_worker(coding, code_key, tiers=["frontier"])
   228	    journal_dir = tmp_path / "journals"
   229	    journal_dir.mkdir()
   230	    state.wire(
   231	        {Tier.MID: subscription, Tier.FRONTIER: coding},
   232	        journal_dir=journal_dir, judge=False,
   233	    )
   234	
   235	    spec = get_template("software_engineering").instantiate("update artifact.txt")
   236	    run = state.engine.start(spec, context={"goal": "update artifact.txt"})
   237	    run = await state.engine.advance(run.run_id)
   238	    assert run.status is RunStatus.AWAITING_APPROVAL
   239	    assert run.awaiting == "specify"
   240	    assert "seed" in run.completed["explore"].output
   241	    assert "seed" in run.completed["specify"].output
   242	    assert artifact.read_text() == "seed\n"
   243	
   244	    state.engine.approve(run.run_id, "specify")
   245	    run = await state.engine.advance(run.run_id)
   246	    assert run.awaiting == "plan"
   247	    assert artifact.read_text() == "seed\n"
   248	
   249	    state.engine.approve(run.run_id, "plan")
   250	    run = await state.engine.advance(run.run_id)
   251	    assert run.awaiting == "review"
   252	    assert artifact.read_text() == "seed\nimplemented\n"
   253	    evidence = run.completed["verify"].output["criteria"][0]["evidence"]
   254	    assert "implemented" in evidence
   255	    assert run.completed["review"].output == {
   256	        "recommendation": "ship",
   257	        "checks": [
   258	            {"area": "spec", "result": "pass", "evidence": "implemented artifact.txt"},
   259	            {"area": "tests", "result": "pass", "evidence": "verification passed"},
   260	            {"area": "edge cases", "result": "pass", "evidence": "no uncovered requirement"},
   261	            {"area": "plan", "result": "pass", "evidence": "no deviation"},
   262	        ],
   263	        "findings": [],
   264	    }
   265	    assert {record.workspace_root for record in run.completed.values()} == {str(workspace)}
   266	
   267	    state.engine.approve(run.run_id, "review")
   268	    run = await state.engine.advance(run.run_id)
   269	    assert run.status is RunStatus.COMPLETED
   270	
   271	    package = build_package_bytes(spec, run, state.engine.journal(run.run_id).entries())
   272	    with zipfile.ZipFile(io.BytesIO(package)) as archive:
   273	        manifest = json.loads(archive.read("manifest.json"))
   274	        assert {step["workspace_root"] for step in manifest["steps"].values()} == {
   275	            str(workspace)
   276	        }
   277	        workspace_files = [name for name in archive.namelist()
   278	                           if name.startswith("workspace/")]
   279	        assert len(workspace_files) == 1
   280	        assert workspace_files[0].endswith("/artifact.txt")

   318	def test_display_model_placeholder_never_reaches_argv(tmp_path):
   319	    """Regression: empty model -> display name 'codex-cli' leaked into the
   320	    invocation as `-m codex-cli`, which Codex rejects on ChatGPT accounts.
   321	    No override means NO model flag; the CLI uses its own default."""
   322	    ws = tmp_path / "ws"
   323	    for cli, flag in (("codex", "-m"), ("claude", "--model"),
   324	                      ("pi", "--model"), ("opencode", "-m")):
   325	        bare = CodingAgentWorker(f"w-{cli}", cli=cli)
   326	        argv, _ = CLI_ADAPTERS[cli].build(bare, "prompt", ws)
   327	        assert flag not in argv, f"{cli}: placeholder model leaked into argv"
   328	        assert bare.model == f"{cli}-cli"  # display/matrix name still set
   329	
   330	        pinned = CodingAgentWorker(f"w2-{cli}", cli=cli, model="real-model-id")
   331	        argv2, _ = CLI_ADAPTERS[cli].build(pinned, "prompt", ws)
   332	        assert argv2[argv2.index(flag) + 1] == "real-model-id"

   255	async def test_schema_guard_retry_then_error():
   256	    calls = {"n": 0}
   257	
   258	    def flaky(task):
   259	        calls["n"] += 1
   260	        if calls["n"] == 1:
   261	            return {"label": "a"}  # missing confidence
   262	        return {"label": "a", "confidence": 0.9}
   263	
   264	    schema = {
   265	        "type": "object",
   266	        "required": ["label", "confidence"],
   267	        "properties": {"label": {"type": "string"}, "confidence": {"type": "number"}},
   268	    }
   269	    guard = SchemaGuard(ScriptedWorker("s1", flaky))
   270	    task = Task(objective="classify", output_schema=schema)
   271	    result = await guard.run(task)
   272	    assert result.error is None and calls["n"] == 2
   273	    assert result.output["confidence"] == 0.9
   274	
   275	    always_bad = SchemaGuard(ScriptedWorker("s2", lambda t: {"nope": 1}))
   276	    result = await always_bad.run(task)
   277	    assert result.error and result.error.startswith("schema:")
   278	
   279	
   280	async def test_schema_guard_accumulates_tokens_across_retries():
   281	    """F2 (panel 2026-07-09, codex+GLM+kimi undercount): each retry rebound
   282	    `result`, discarding the earlier attempt's tokens/cost, so the budget saw only
   283	    the final attempt. The returned WorkerResult must carry the SUM of every
   284	    attempt (mirroring SelfConsistency/SelfCritique)."""
   285	    from metaharness.core.budget import Budget
   286	
   287	    schema = {"type": "object", "required": ["label"],
   288	              "properties": {"label": {"type": "string"}}}
   289	    calls = {"n": 0}
   290	
   291	    def flaky(task):
   292	        calls["n"] += 1
   293	        return {} if calls["n"] == 1 else {"label": "a"}  # invalid, then valid
   294	
   295	    class Billed(ScriptedWorker):
   296	        async def _execute(self, task):
   297	            r = await super()._execute(task)
   298	            r.tokens_in, r.tokens_out, r.cost_usd = 100, 50, 0.01
   299	            return r
   300	
   301	    guard = SchemaGuard(Billed("s", flaky))
   302	    result = await guard.run(Task(objective="classify", output_schema=schema))
   303	    assert result.error is None and calls["n"] == 2
   304	    assert result.tokens_in == 200 and result.tokens_out == 100   # both attempts summed
   305	    assert result.cost_usd == pytest.approx(0.02)
   306	
   307	    budget = Budget()
   308	    budget.charge(cost_usd=result.cost_usd, tokens=result.tokens_in + result.tokens_out)
   309	    assert budget.spent_tokens == 300
   310

   326	
   327	async def test_self_critique_runs_draft_critique_revise():
   328	    from metaharness.harness import SelfCritique
   329	
   330	    calls = []
     1	"""Subscription-CLI workers: LLM access through logged-in coding CLIs.
     2	
     3	Claude Code (`claude -p`) rides an Anthropic subscription; Codex CLI
     4	(`codex exec`) rides a ChatGPT/OpenAI one. Both answer arbitrary text tasks
     5	headless, so a signed-in CLI is a legitimate LLM provider — no API key stored,
     6	no per-token bill. The CLI's own auth store is the credential; the harness
     7	never sees it.
     8	
     9	Mechanically these reuse the CodingAgentWorker adapters (same one-shot
    10	invocation, same parsers) with two differences: the harness binds them to its
    11	active workspace during wiring, and their CLI tools are read-only — a
    12	subscription LLM worker must inspect and answer, not edit.
    13	"""
    14	from __future__ import annotations
    15	
    16	import shutil
    17	from pathlib import Path
    18	from typing import Any, Optional
    19	
    20	from metaharness.core.types import Tier
    21	from metaharness.harness.coding import CodingAgentWorker
    22	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    23	
    24	# model aliases the CLIs accept; "" = the CLI's configured default
    25	SUBSCRIPTION_CLIS: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {
    26	    "claude": {
    27	        "label": "Claude Code (Anthropic subscription)",
    28	        "binary": "claude",
    29	        "auth_paths": ["~/.claude.json", "~/.claude"],
    30	        "login_hint": "run `claude` once and sign in, or `claude login`",
    31	        "models": ["sonnet", "opus", "haiku", "claude-fable-5", "claude-opus-4-8"],
    32	    },
    33	    "codex": {
    34	        "label": "Codex CLI (OpenAI subscription)",
    35	        "binary": "codex",
    36	        "auth_paths": ["~/.codex/auth.json"],
    37	        "login_hint": "run `codex login` and sign in with ChatGPT",
    38	        "models": ["gpt-5.2-codex", "gpt-5.2", "o5"],
    39	    },
    40	}
    41	
    42	
    43	def subscription_status() -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
    44	    """Install + sign-in state per subscription CLI, for the Settings view.
    45	    Auth detection is a file heuristic (same approach as structure-discovery-
    46	    lab): it can say 'signed in' wrongly after a logout, but the wizard's live
    47	    Test button is the real check."""
    48	    status = {}
    49	    for name, spec in SUBSCRIPTION_CLIS.items():
    50	        path = shutil.which(spec["binary"])
    51	        authenticated = any(
    52	            Path(p).expanduser().exists() for p in spec["auth_paths"]
    53	        ) if path else False
    54	        status[name] = {
    55	            "label": spec["label"],
    56	            "installed": path is not None,
    57	            "path": path,
    58	            "authenticated": authenticated,
    59	            "login_hint": spec["login_hint"],
    60	            "models": spec["models"],
    61	        }
    62	    return status
    63	
    64	
    65	class SubscriptionWorker(CodingAgentWorker):
    66	    """A tier worker whose completions come from a signed-in CLI."""
    67	
    68	    BASE_TIMEOUT_S = 300.0  # answer-only calls need less room than CodingAgentWorker's edits
    69	
    70	    def __init__(
    71	        self,
    72	        worker_id: str,
    73	        cli: str,
    74	        model: str = "",
    75	        tier: Tier = Tier.FRONTIER,
    76	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
    77	        system_prompt: str = "",
    78	        workspace: Optional[Path] = None,
    79	        timeout_s: Optional[float] = None,  # None = task-type-aware default (issue #2)
    80	        **kwargs: Any,
    81	    ) -> None:
    82	        if cli not in SUBSCRIPTION_CLIS:
    83	            raise ValueError(
    84	                f"unknown subscription CLI {cli!r} (known: {sorted(SUBSCRIPTION_CLIS)})")
    85	        timeout_kwargs = {} if timeout_s is None else {"timeout_s": timeout_s}
    86	        super().__init__(
    87	            worker_id,
    88	            cli=cli,
    89	            model=model,
    90	            tier=tier,
    91	            keypair=keypair,
    92	            system_prompt=system_prompt,
    93	            workspace=workspace,
    94	            **timeout_kwargs,
    95	            **kwargs,
    96	        )
    97	        # answer, don't edit: Codex gets its read-only sandbox; Claude's adapter
    98	        # restricts it to plan mode with Read/Glob/Grep only.
    99	        self.sandbox = "read-only"
   100	        A code-carrying candidate (`code_ref` set) wraps the knob stack with a
   101	        CODE artifact loaded from `ledger_root / code_ref`, applied OUTERMOST so
   102	        it sees the fully-composed knob stack. `ledger_root` is REQUIRED when
   103	        `code_ref` is set — build runs from three places (evaluation, serve-boot
   104	        promotion apply, web approval) and a cwd-relative resolve would silently
   105	        load the wrong file, so we refuse rather than guess."""
   106	        runner = base
   107	        if self.tool_offload:
   108	            runner = ToolOffload(runner)
   109	        if self.self_consistency_k > 1:
   110	            runner = SelfConsistency(runner, k=self.self_consistency_k)
   111	        if self.schema_guard_retries > 0:
   112	            runner = SchemaGuard(runner, max_retries=self.schema_guard_retries)
   113	        if self.self_critique_rounds > 0:
   114	            runner = SelfCritique(runner, rounds=self.self_critique_rounds)
   115	        if self.prompt_directives:
   116	            runner = PromptDirectives(runner, self.prompt_directives)
   117	        if self.code_ref is not None:
   118	            runner = self._load_code_module(ledger_root).build(runner)
   119	        return runner
   120	
   121	    def _load_code_module(self, ledger_root: Path | None):
   122	        """Resolve and import this candidate's code artifact, returning the
   123	        module (which must expose a callable `build`). Refuses to resolve
   124	        without a ledger_root, enforces realpath containment under the root
   125	        (symlink-escape safe), and wraps every load failure in a RuntimeError
   126	        that names the code_ref."""
   127	        if ledger_root is None:
   128	            raise ValueError("code-backed params require ledger_root")
   129	        root = Path(ledger_root).resolve()
   130	        target = (root / self.code_ref).resolve()
   131	        if not target.is_relative_to(root):
   132	            raise RuntimeError(
   133	                f"code_ref {self.code_ref!r} resolves outside the ledger root"
   134	            )
   135	        if not target.is_file():
   136	            raise RuntimeError(f"code_ref {self.code_ref!r} is not a file: {target}")
   137	        # F4 (panel 2026-07-09, codex P1 + GLM P3 + kimi P2 + opus, TOCTOU/trust):
   138	        # when a code_hash was recorded, the bytes on disk must still match it, or
   139	        # a candidate's own code (or a later round) could rewrite the file and get
   140	        # unscored bytes promoted/run under a stale hash. Verify before importing.
   141	        if self.code_hash is not None:
   142	            import hashlib
   143	
   144	            actual = hashlib.sha256(target.read_bytes()).hexdigest()
   145	            if actual != self.code_hash:
   146	                raise RuntimeError(
   147	                    f"code artifact does not match recorded hash for code_ref "
   148	                    f"{self.code_ref!r} (expected {self.code_hash}, got {actual})"
   149	                )
   150	        spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(f"metaharness_code::{target}", target)
   151	        if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
   152	            raise RuntimeError(f"code_ref {self.code_ref!r} could not be loaded as a module")
   153	        module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
   154	        try:
   155	            spec.loader.exec_module(module)
   156	        except Exception as exc:  # any import-time error, named for the ledger
   157	            raise RuntimeError(f"code_ref {self.code_ref!r} failed to import: {exc}") from exc
   158	        if not callable(getattr(module, "build", None)):
   159	            raise RuntimeError(
   160	                f"code_ref {self.code_ref!r} defines no callable build(base) -> Runner"
   161	            )
   162	        return module
   163	
   164	
   165	class PromptDirectives(_Wrapper):
   166	    """Additive prompt-space search: append candidate directives to the task's
   167	    boundaries (the delegation contract) without touching anything else."""
   168	
   169	    def __init__(self, inner: Runner, directives: list[str]) -> None:
   170	        super().__init__(inner)
   171	        self.directives = list(directives)
   172	
   173	    async def run(self, task):
   174	        amended = task.model_copy(deep=True)
   175	        amended.boundaries = list(task.boundaries) + self.directives
   176	        result = await self.inner.run(amended)
   177	        result.task_id = task.id
   178	        return result
   179	
   180	
   181	# Knob documentation handed to the LLM proposer — kept next to the fields so a
   182	# new knob can't ship without the proposer learning it exists.
   183	KNOB_DOCS = """\
   184	Tunable knobs (the delta may set any subset):
   185	- tool_offload (bool): PAL — arithmetic tasks emit a program that is evaluated
   186	  exactly instead of computed by the model. Helps when arithmetic answers are wrong.
   187	- self_consistency_k (int, 1..7): sample k answers, majority-vote. Helps when wrong
   188	  answers scatter across attempts. Multiplies token cost by ~k.
   189	- schema_guard_retries (int, 0..3): re-ask naming schema violations. Helps when

     1	"""Grounded reflection: turn a failed attempt into advice for the next one.
     2	
     3	The research consensus is blunt: intrinsic self-correction ("think again") doesn't
     4	work; reflection helps only when grounded in an external signal (CRITIC, Reflexion).
     5	So this reflector speaks only from the verifier's evidence — and it deliberately
     6	does NOT leak the expected answer for equality checks, because "the answer is X"
     7	isn't learning, it's dictation. Spec-level requirements (schema shape, required
     8	substring) are fair game: the worker was already entitled to them.
     9	
    10	Framing note (arXiv 2606.05976, "The Self-Correction Illusion"): models refute an
    11	erroneous claim far more reliably when it is presented as an external, addressable
    12	artifact than as their own prior thought. Reflections therefore describe "a
    13	previous attempt" in the third person — never "you were wrong" — and arrive via
    14	the task contract's boundaries, i.e. an external role.
    15	"""
    16	from __future__ import annotations
    17	
    18	from typing import Optional
    19	
    20	from metaharness.core.types import Attempt, MASTMode, Task, Verdict
    21	
    22	
    23	def grounded_reflector(task: Task, attempt: Attempt) -> Optional[str]:
    24	    verification = attempt.verification
    25	    if verification.verdict != Verdict.FAIL:
    26	        return None
    27	    mode = verification.failure_mode
    28	
    29	    if mode == MASTMode.SCHEMA_INVALID:
    30	        return (
    31	            f"A previous attempt at this task violated the required schema: "
    32	            f"{verification.detail}. Return output that matches the schema exactly — "
    33	            "every required key, correct types."
    34	        )
    35	    if mode == MASTMode.TOOL_ERROR:
    36	        return (
    37	            f"A previous attempt failed with an execution error: {verification.detail}. "
    38	            "Simplify the approach and avoid whatever triggered the error."
    39	        )
    40	    if mode == MASTMode.TIMEOUT:
    41	        # advice must fit what a retry can do — raising the timeout is a
    42	        # config action, not something the worker itself can choose (issue #2)
    43	        return (
    44	            "A previous attempt ran out of time before finishing. Take the most "
    45	            "direct path to the objective and keep the change minimal."
    46	        )
    47	    if mode == MASTMode.BUDGET_EXCEEDED:
    48	        return None  # no next attempt is coming; advice would be noise
    49	    if verification.scorer == "execution":
    50	        # Issue #1: a workspace test is stronger than any text success_check.
    51	        # Preserve its concrete diagnostic instead of falling into the equals /
    52	        # contains branches below and telling the retry to fix narration.
    53	        return (
    54	            "A previous code change failed its workspace test suite: "
    55	            f"{verification.detail}. Fix the failing behavior, then rerun the tests."
    56	        )
    57	
    58	    check = task.success_check or {}
    59	    if "contains" in check:
    60	        return (
    61	            f"A previous attempt was rejected because its output did not include the "
    62	            f"required content {check['contains']!r}. Make sure it appears explicitly."
    63	        )
    64	    if "one_of" in check:
    65	        return (
    66	            f"A previous attempt returned {attempt.result.output!r}, which is not one "
    67	            f"of the allowed values {check['one_of']!r}. Choose exactly one of them."
    68	        )
    69	    if "equals" in check:
    70	        # grounded but not leaked: name what was wrong, not what is right
    71	        return (
    72	            f"A previous attempt returned {attempt.result.output!r}; the verifier "
    73	            "checked it against the task's expected result and rejected it. "
    74	            "Re-read the objective and inputs, reason step by step, and answer again."
    75	        )
    76	    return (
    77	        f"A previous attempt failed verification: {verification.detail or 'no detail'}. "
    78	        "Take a materially different approach."
    79	    )

     2	
     3	``TaskExecutor`` already accepts a ``playbook_hints`` callable that feeds

    41	# emitted the same embedder_id, invisible to reindex_needed). Re-exported
    42	# here so existing imports keep working.
    43	from selflearn.ports import OpenAICompatEmbedding  # noqa: E402,F401

    49	def record_qualification(matrix, qualification, task_types=("general",)) -> None:
    50	    """Record a selflearn QualificationResult as capability evidence.
    51	
    52	    The matrix keys evidence by (model, task_type); a pack qualification
    53	    lands as evidence for the task types the pack's specialists serve, so
    54	    routing learns which models are worth handing that domain."""
    55	    from metaharness.core.types import TaskType
    56	
    57	    for task_type in task_types:
    58	        matrix.record(qualification.model_id, TaskType(task_type),
    59	                      qualification.qualified)

    61	
    62	def make_knowledge_hints(
    63	    store,
    64	    specs: Sequence,
    65	    embedder=None,
    66	    index: bool = True,
    67	) -> Callable[[Task], list[str]]:
    68	    """Build a ``playbook_hints``-shaped callable from specialist specs.
    69	
    70	    ``store`` is a selflearn PackStore and ``specs`` are selflearn
    71	    SpecialistSpec objects (typed loosely here so this module imports even
    72	    when selflearn is absent; construction requires it via the retriever).
    73	    Each call retrieves per the first spec serving the task's type and
    74	    renders one fenced injection block, or returns no advice.
    75	    """
    76	    from selflearn.retrieval import Retriever, render_injection_block
    77	
    78	    retriever = Retriever(store, embedder)
    79	    if index and embedder is not None:
    80	        for spec in specs:
    81	            for pack in spec.packs:
    82	                retriever.index(pack)
    83	
    84	    def hints(task: Task) -> list[str]:
    85	        task_type = getattr(task.task_type, "value", str(task.task_type))
    86	        spec = next((s for s in specs if s.serves(task_type)), None)
    87	        if spec is None:
    88	            return []
    89	        results = retriever.retrieve(list(spec.packs), task.objective,
    90	                                     k=spec.retrieval_k,
    91	                                     budget_tokens=spec.retrieval_budget_tokens,
    92	                                     task_type=task_type)
    93	        block = render_injection_block(results)
    94	        return [] if block.empty else [block.text]
    95	
    96	    return hints
     1	"""Knowledge-driven planning (plan decision 10): before the LLM planner
     2	runs, check whether a published workflow-kind entry already knows how to
     3	structure this goal.
     4	
     5	Strong semantic match → the entry's ``procedure:`` compiles deterministically
     6	into a WorkflowSpec (no LLM in the loop, checks derived by the existing
     7	engine machinery). Weak match → the entry's prose returns as planning
     8	guidance for the normal planner. No match → nothing changes.
     9	
    10	Param filling for ``{placeholders}`` in step objectives is a named
    11	knowledge-scout step (simulation finding 5) — until M5 wires it, the goal
    12	itself is appended to each step objective so instantiation stays useful
    13	without invented parameter values.
    14	"""
    15	from __future__ import annotations
    16	
    17	from typing import Optional, Sequence
    18	
    19	from metaharness.core.types import TaskType
    20	from metaharness.workflows.dsl import WorkflowSpec
    21	
    22	STRONG_MATCH_SCORE = 0.15
    23	
    24	_VALID_TASK_TYPES = {t.value for t in TaskType}
    25	
    26	
    27	def plan_from_knowledge(
    28	    goal: str,
    29	    store,
    30	    packs: Sequence[str],
    31	    embedder,
    32	) -> tuple[Optional[WorkflowSpec], str, str]:
    33	    """Returns (spec, seeded_by, guidance).
    34	
    35	    spec is a deterministic WorkflowSpec when a workflow entry matched
    36	    strongly (seeded_by = its entry id); otherwise spec is None and guidance
    37	    carries the best weak match's prose ("" when no workflow entries exist).
    38	
    39	    Plan-level marks: record the returned seeded_by id in
    40	    ``TaskOutcome.seeded_by`` on every step outcome of the instantiated run
    41	    — a verified pass credits it (helpful), and a failing step may implicate
    42	    it (harmful) even though it was never injected into a prompt, because
    43	    it shaped the plan itself.
    44	    """
    45	    from selflearn.retrieval import Retriever
    46	
    47	    retriever = Retriever(store, embedder)
    48	    if embedder is not None:
    49	        for pack in packs:
    50	            retriever.index(pack)
    51	    results = retriever.retrieve(list(packs), goal, k=8, budget_tokens=100000)
    52	    workflows = [r for r in results if r.entry.cand.kind == "workflow"]
    53	    if not workflows:
    54	        return None, "", ""
    55	    best = workflows[0]
    56	    if best.score < STRONG_MATCH_SCORE:
    57	        return (None, best.entry_id,
    58	                f"Planning guidance from {best.entry_id} (weak match):\n"
    59	                f"{best.entry.cand.body}")
    60	
    61	    cand = best.entry.cand
    62	    steps = []
    63	    for step in cand.procedure:
    64	        task_type = (step.task_type if step.task_type in _VALID_TASK_TYPES
    65	                     else TaskType.GENERAL.value)
    66	        inputs = {"goal": "$context.goal"}
    67	        for dep in step.depends_on:
    68	            inputs[dep] = f"$steps.{dep}.output"
    69	        steps.append({
    70	            "id": step.id,
    71	            "task_type": task_type,
    72	            "objective": f"{step.objective}\nGoal: {goal}",
    73	            "inputs": inputs,
    74	            "boundaries": [f"Seeded by knowledge entry {cand.id}; per-step "
    75	                           f"check: {step.check_dict() or 'none declared'}"],
    76	            "tools": list(step.tools),
    77	            "depends_on": list(step.depends_on),
    78	        })
    79	    spec = WorkflowSpec.model_validate({
    80	        "name": f"knowledge:{cand.id}"[:60],
    81	        "steps": steps,
    82	    })
    83	    return spec, cand.id, ""

     1	"""Tool registry: one catalog of everything a worker may call — builtin tools
     2	and MCP-server tools — plus the selection logic that keeps per-step tool
     3	subsets SMALL.
     4	
     5	Design per memory/knowledge_base/context-engineering-agent-harnesses.md:
     6	- workers never see the full catalog: accuracy degrades with tool count, and
     7	  small local models degrade worst (RAG-MCP, MCPVerse). `select_for` returns
     8	  an adaptive shortlist (score cliff, cap 7).
     9	- schemas render deterministically (sorted keys, stable order) so a worker's
    10	  prompt prefix stays KV-cache-friendly across rounds.
    11	- tool RESULTS are pruned before they re-enter context: task-conditioned
    12	  digest with head/tail preserved (Squeez-style), never a silent truncation.
    13	"""
    14	from __future__ import annotations
    15	
    16	import inspect
    17	import hashlib
    18	import json
    19	import re
    20	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    21	from typing import Any, Callable, Optional
    22	
    23	from metaharness.observability.run_events import emit_run_event
    24	
    25	MAX_RESULT_CHARS = 4_000
    26	DEFAULT_SUBSET_CAP = 7
    27	
    28	
    29	@dataclass
    30	class ToolSpec:
    31	    name: str
    32	    description: str
    33	    input_schema: dict[str, Any]                  # JSON schema for arguments
    34	    handler: Callable[..., Any]                   # sync or async; kwargs from args
    35	    source: str = "builtin"                       # builtin | mcp:<server>
    36	    keywords: tuple[str, ...] = ()                # extra terms for selection
    37	    annotations: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)  # MCP safety hints
    38	
    39	
    40	class ToolError(Exception):
    41	    """A tool failed; the message is worker-visible data, never instructions."""
    42	
    43	
    44	_WORD_RE = re.compile(r"[a-z0-9_]+")
    45	
    46	
    47	def _terms(text: str) -> set[str]:
    48	    return set(_WORD_RE.findall(text.lower()))
    49	
    50	
    51	def digest_text(text: str, max_chars: int = MAX_RESULT_CHARS,
    52	                focus_terms: Optional[set[str]] = None) -> str:
    53	    """Shrink a blob to budget, keeping focus-relevant lines plus head/tail.
    54	    The pruning is always LOUD — the reader sees exactly what was dropped."""
    55	    if len(text) <= max_chars:
    56	        return text
    57	    focus_terms = focus_terms or set()
    58	    kept: list[str] = []
    59	    used = 0
    60	    focus_budget = max_chars // 2
    61	    if focus_terms:
    62	        for line in text.splitlines():
    63	            if _terms(line) & focus_terms and used + len(line) < focus_budget:
    64	                kept.append(line)
    65	                used += len(line) + 1
    66	    remainder = max_chars - used
    67	    head = text[: int(remainder * 0.7)]
    68	    tail = text[-int(remainder * 0.3):] if remainder > 10 else ""
    69	    dropped = len(text) - used - len(head) - len(tail)
    70	    parts = [head, f"\n[…pruned {dropped} chars…]\n", tail]
    71	    if kept:
    72	        parts += ["\n[objective-relevant lines kept:]\n", "\n".join(kept)]
    73	    return "".join(parts)
    74	
    75	
    76	class ToolRegistry:
    77	    def __init__(self) -> None:
    78	        self._tools: dict[str, ToolSpec] = {}
    79	        # the jail root of this registry's file tools ("" = no file tools);
    80	        # workers stamp it onto WorkerResult.workspace_root so downstream
    81	        # consumers know where file side-effects actually landed
    82	        self.workspace_root: str = ""
    83	
    84	    def register(self, spec: ToolSpec) -> None:
    85	        if spec.name in self._tools:
    86	            raise ValueError(f"tool {spec.name!r} already registered")
    87	        self._tools[spec.name] = spec
    88	
    89	    def unregister_source(self, source: str) -> int:
    90	        """Drop every tool from one source (e.g. an MCP server being reloaded)."""
    91	        names = [n for n, t in self._tools.items() if t.source == source]
    92	        for name in names:
    93	            del self._tools[name]
    94	        return len(names)
    95	
    96	    def get(self, name: str) -> Optional[ToolSpec]:
    97	        return self._tools.get(name)
    98	
    99	    def all(self) -> list[ToolSpec]:
   100	        return [self._tools[n] for n in sorted(self._tools)]
   101	
   102	    def names(self) -> list[str]:
   103	        return sorted(self._tools)
   104	
   105	    # ------------------------------------------------------------- selection
   106	
   107	    def select_for(self, objective: str, boundaries: Optional[list[str]] = None,
   108	                   cap: int = DEFAULT_SUBSET_CAP) -> list[str]:
   109	        """Adaptive tool shortlist for one step: score by term overlap
   110	        (name 3x, keywords 2x, description 1x), keep tools above a cliff
   111	        relative to the best score, cap the subset. No signal -> NO tools;
   112	        most steps are pure text-work and tools would only confuse."""
   113	        text_terms = _terms(objective + " " + " ".join(boundaries or []))
   114	        scored: list[tuple[float, str]] = []
   115	        for name, tool in self._tools.items():
   116	            score = (
   117	                3.0 * len(text_terms & _terms(tool.name.replace(".", " ")))
   118	                + 2.0 * len(text_terms & _terms(" ".join(tool.keywords)))
   119	                + 1.0 * len(text_terms & _terms(tool.description))
   120	            )
   121	            if score > 0:
   122	                scored.append((score, name))
   123	        if not scored:
   124	            return []
   125	        scored.sort(key=lambda pair: (-pair[0], pair[1]))
   126	        top = scored[0][0]
   127	        cliff = max(2.0, 0.4 * top)
   128	        return [name for score, name in scored[:cap] if score >= cliff]
   129	
   130	    # -------------------------------------------------------------- schemas
   131	
   132	    def openai_schemas(self, names: list[str]) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   133	        """OpenAI function-calling schemas, deterministic order & serialization
   134	        (sorted by name; sorted keys downstream keeps the prefix byte-stable)."""
   135	        schemas = []
   136	        for name in sorted(set(names)):
   137	            tool = self._tools.get(name)
   138	            if tool is None:
   139	                continue  # a plan may reference a tool that has since unloaded
   140	            schemas.append({
   141	                "type": "function",
   142	                "function": {
   143	                    "name": tool.name.replace(".", "__"),  # dialect-safe name
   144	                    "description": tool.description,
   145	                    "parameters": tool.input_schema,
   146	                },
   147	            })
   148	        return schemas
   149	
   150	    def resolve_call_name(self, wire_name: str) -> Optional[str]:
   151	        """Map a dialect-safe wire name (dots escaped) back to the registry."""
   152	        if wire_name in self._tools:
   153	            return wire_name
   154	        dotted = wire_name.replace("__", ".")
   155	        return dotted if dotted in self._tools else None
   156	
   157	    # ------------------------------------------------------------ execution
   158	
   159	    async def call(self, name: str, arguments: dict[str, Any],
   160	                   focus: str = "") -> str:
   161	        """Run a tool; the return value is a pruned STRING (worker-facing).
   162	        Errors come back as data ('tool error: …') so the worker can adapt,
   163	        while a missing tool is a hard error — that's a harness bug."""
   164	        resolved = self.resolve_call_name(name)
   165	        if resolved is None:
   166	            raise ToolError(f"unknown tool {name!r}")
   167	        tool = self._tools[resolved]
   168	        # Stable, non-secret request identity: enough for approval/audit layers
   169	        # to correlate retries without copying argument values into journals.
   170	        request_bytes = json.dumps(
   171	            {"tool": resolved, "arguments": arguments}, sort_keys=True,
   172	            ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"), default=str,
   173	        ).encode("utf-8")
   174	        request_id = hashlib.sha256(request_bytes).hexdigest()
   175	        request_event = {
   176	            "tool": resolved,
   177	            "request_id": request_id,
   178	            "idempotency_key": request_id,
   179	            "argument_keys": sorted(str(key) for key in arguments),
   180	        }
   181	        emit_run_event("tool.requested", request_event)
   182	        try:
   183	            result = tool.handler(**arguments)
   184	            if inspect.isawaitable(result):
   185	                result = await result
   186	        except ToolError as exc:
   187	            result = f"tool error: {exc}"
   188	            emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "error"})
   189	            return result
   190	        except TypeError as exc:  # bad/missing arguments — worker can retry
   191	            result = f"tool error: bad arguments for {resolved}: {exc}"
   192	            emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "error"})
   193	            return result
   194	        except Exception:
   195	            emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "error"})
   196	            raise
   197	        if not isinstance(result, str):
   198	            result = json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, default=str, sort_keys=True)
   199	        emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "completed"})
   200	        return digest_text(result, MAX_RESULT_CHARS, _terms(focus))

    34	def test_canonical_json_is_key_order_independent_and_stable():
    35	    a = {"z": 1, "a": {"y": 2, "x": [3, 2, 1]}}
    36	    b = {"a": {"x": [3, 2, 1], "y": 2}, "z": 1}
    37	    assert canonical_json(a) == canonical_json(b)
    38	    assert content_hash(a) == content_hash(b)
    39	    assert canonical_json(a) == canonical_json(json.loads(canonical_json(a)))

    42	def test_content_hash_changes_with_any_semantic_difference():
    43	    base = {"role": "user", "content": "hello"}
    44	    mutated = {"role": "user", "content": "Hello"}
    45	    assert content_hash(base) != content_hash(mutated)
    46	    assert content_hash("hello") != content_hash({"content": "hello"})

    49	def test_fit_receipt_manifest_hash_is_reproducible_across_independent_calls():
    50	    secret = "unique-redaction-marker-77421"
    51	    messages = [
    52	        {"role": "system", "content": "contract " * 20},
    53	        {"role": "user", "content": f"detail {secret} " * 50},
    54	        {"role": "user", "content": "final response contract"},
    55	    ]
    56	    first = fit_messages_with_receipt(
    57	        copy.deepcopy(messages),
    58	        budget_tokens=400,
    59	        model_id="m",
    60	        harness_version="h",
    61	        redaction_values=[secret],
    62	        tool_schemas=[{"type": "function", "function": {"name": "read", "parameters": {}}}],
    63	    )
    64	    second = fit_messages_with_receipt(
    65	        copy.deepcopy(messages),
    66	        budget_tokens=400,
    67	        model_id="m",
    68	        harness_version="h",
    69	        redaction_values=[secret],
    70	        tool_schemas=[{"type": "function", "function": {"name": "read", "parameters": {}}}],
    71	    )
    72	    assert first.manifest.manifest_hash == second.manifest.manifest_hash
    73	    assert first.envelope.content_hash == second.envelope.content_hash
    74	    assert first.manifest.model_dump_json() == second.manifest.model_dump_json()

    77	@pytest.mark.parametrize("tier", [Tier.SMALL, Tier.MID, Tier.FRONTIER])
    78	def test_section_budget_allocation_is_deterministic_and_exhaustive(tier):
    79	    from metaharness.context import ContextSectionType
    80	
    81	    sections = [
    82	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
    83	        ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT,
    84	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY,
    85	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
    86	        ContextSectionType.TOOL_SCHEMAS,
    87	    ]
    88	    first = allocate_section_budgets(sections, 977, tier)
    89	    second = allocate_section_budgets(sections, 977, tier)
    90	    assert first == second
    91	    assert sum(first) == 977
    92	    assert all(value >= 0 for value in first)

   119	            after_hash=same_hash,

   121	            final_tokens=4,

   143	    secret = "sk-super-secret-value-0000000000"
   144	    messages = [
   145	        {"role": "system", "content": "system"},
   146	        {
   147	            "role": "user",

   151	                    secret: "value-under-a-secret-key",
   152	                }
   153	            ),
   154	        },
   155	    ]

   157	    receipt = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   158	        messages,
   159	        budget_tokens=10_000,
   160	        model_id="m",
   161	        harness_version="h",
   162	        redaction_values=[secret],
   163	    )
   164	    assert messages == original
   165	    persisted = receipt.manifest.model_dump_json()

     3	Every test here exercises behavior that src/metaharness/context enforces

     7	scope isolation, artifact-ref packaging completeness), see
     8	test_memory_skill_boundaries.py.

    31	def test_corpus_is_well_formed_and_covers_every_required_category():
    32	    from tests.adversarial._meta5_support import load_corpus
    33	
    34	    corpus = load_corpus()
    35	    required_categories = {
    36	        "unknown_operations",
    37	        "traversal",
    38	        "cross_scope_access",
    39	        "immutable_evidence_rewrites",
    40	        "premature_logging",
    41	        "lossy_compression",
    42	        "activation_or_tombstoning",
    43	        "specialist_task_actions",
    44	        "unreceipted_mutation",
    45	        "task_action_training_targets",
    46	        "hw_confounding",
    47	        "repeated_set_promotion",
    48	        "incompatible_reuse",
    49	        "unhealthy_fallback",
    50	        "incomplete_packaging",
    51	        "evaluator_non_self_approval",
    52	    }
    53	    assert required_categories.issubset(set(corpus["categories"]))
    54	    seen_categories = {case["category"] for case in corpus["cases"]}
    55	    assert required_categories.issubset(seen_categories)
    56	
    57	    seen_ids = [case["id"] for case in corpus["cases"]]
    58	    assert len(seen_ids) == len(set(seen_ids)), "case ids must be unique"
    59	
    60	    requirement_ids = [case["requirement_id"] for case in corpus["cases"] if case["requirement_id"]]
    61	    for req_id in requirement_ids:
    62	        assert req_id.startswith("META5-MEM-"), req_id
    63	    # Every requirement id in the corpus must be a member of the documented
    64	    # META5-MEM card set (META5-MEM-001 .. META5-MEM-015). The cardinality
    65	    # of the *currently* absent set is asserted by
    66	    # test_all_absent_cases_have_a_stable_requirement_id_and_a_test_below
    67	    # in tests/adversarial/test_memory_skill_boundaries.py and shrinks as
    68	    # stages flip cards to enforced; this corpus-shape check is the global
    69	    # "no stray requirement ids" guard.
    70	    documented_metakernel_cards = {f"META5-MEM-{number:03d}" for number in range(1, 16)}
    71	    assert set(requirement_ids).issubset(documented_metakernel_cards)
    72	
    73	    for case in corpus["cases"]:
    74	        if case["status"] == "enforced":
    75	            assert case["requirement_id"] is None, case["id"]
    76	        if case["status"] == "absent":
    77	            assert case["requirement_id"] is not None, case["id"]
    78	            assert case["suite"] == "test_memory_skill_boundaries", case["id"]
    79

     1	"""META-5: executable negative tests for provenance/authority and immutability.

    58
